##### **From Prototype to Classroom: An Intelligent Tutoring System for Quantum Education**
2604.24807v1 by Iizalaarab Elhaimeur, Nikos Chrisochoides

Quantum computing instructors face a compounding problem: the concepts are counterintuitive, the mathematical formalism is dense, and qualified faculty are scarce outside a small number of well-resourced institutions. Our prior work introduced a knowledge-graph-augmented tutoring prototype with two specialized LLM agents: a Teaching Agent for dynamic interaction and a Lesson Planning Agent for lesson generation. Validated on simulated runs rather than in a real course, that prototype left open whether more aggressive agent specialization would be needed to handle the full range of quantum education tasks under real student load. This paper answers the three questions that the prototype could not answer. Can agent specialization solve the reliability problem in a domain as technically demanding as quantum information science? Can the system run in a real course, not a demonstration? Does the instructor gain actionable intelligence from the deployment? We present ITAS (Intelligent Teaching Assistant System), a multi-agent tutoring system built around four contributions: a five-module QIS curriculum grounded in Watrous's information-first framework, a Spoke-and-Wheel teaching architecture with quantum-specialized agents, a cloud infrastructure designed for production use and regulatory compliance, and a conversational analytics layer for instructors and content developers. Piloted in a quantum computing course at Old Dominion University, the system supports all three answers: deployment evidence is consistent with specialization addressing the task-boundary failures observed in the prototype, cloud infrastructure supports classroom-scale concurrency at sub-textbook cost, and the analytics agent surfaces curriculum gaps the instructor could not otherwise see.

摘要：量子計算的教師面臨一個複雜的問題：這些概念違反直覺，數學形式主義密集，並且合格的教職員在少數資源豐富的機構之外相當稀缺。我們之前的工作介紹了一個知識圖譜增強的輔導原型，該原型有兩個專門的 LLM 代理：一個用於動態互動的教學代理和一個用於課程生成的課程規劃代理。該原型在模擬運行中進行驗證，而不是在真實課程中，這讓人懷疑是否需要更積極的代理專業化來處理在真實學生負載下的全範圍量子教育任務。本文回答了該原型無法回答的三個問題。代理專業化能否解決在量子信息科學這樣技術要求高的領域中的可靠性問題？系統能否在真實課程中運行，而不是演示？教師能否從部署中獲得可行的情報？我們提出了 ITAS（智能教學助手系統），這是一個多代理輔導系統，圍繞四個貢獻構建：基於 Watrous 的信息優先框架的五模塊 QIS 課程，一個具有量子專門代理的輻射式教學架構，設計用於生產使用和合規的雲基礎設施，以及為教師和內容開發者提供的對話分析層。該系統在老道明大學的量子計算課程中進行了試點，支持所有三個答案：部署證據與專業化解決原型中觀察到的任務邊界失敗一致，雲基礎設施支持課堂規模的並發運行，成本低於教科書，並且分析代理揭示了教師無法看到的課程空白。

##### **Factual and Edit-Sensitive Graph-to-Sequence Generation via Graph-Aware Adaptive Noising**
2604.24104v1 by Aditya Hemant Shahane, Anuj Kumar Sirohi, Tanmoy Chakraborty, Prathosh A P, Sandeep Kumar

Fine-tuned autoregressive models for graph-to-sequence generation (G2S) often struggle with factual grounding and edit sensitivity. To tackle these issues, we propose a non-autoregressive diffusion framework that generates text by iterative refinement conditioned on an input graph, named as Diffusion Language Model for Graphs (DLM4G). By aligning graph components (entities/relations) with their corresponding sequence tokens, DLM4G employs an adaptive noising strategy. The proposed strategy uses per-token denoising error as a signal to adaptively modulate noise on entity and relation tokens, improving preservation of graph structure and enabling localized updates under graph edits. Evaluated on three datasets, DLM4G consistently outperforms competitive G2S diffusion baselines trained on identical splits across both surface-form and embedding-based metrics. DLM4G further exceeds fine-tuned autoregressive baselines up to 12x larger (e.g., T5-Large) and is competitive with zero-shot LLM transfer baselines up to 127x larger. Relative to the strongest fine-tuned PLM baseline, DLM4G improves factual grounding (FGT@0.5) by +5.16% and edit sensitivity (ESR) by +7.9%; compared to the best diffusion baseline, it yields gains of +3.75% in FGT@0.5 and +23.6% in ESR. We additionally demonstrate applicability beyond textual graphs through experiments on molecule captioning, indicating the method's generality for scientific G2S generation.

摘要：微調的自回歸模型在圖到序列生成（G2S）中常常面臨事實基礎和編輯敏感性問題。為了解決這些問題，我們提出了一種非自回歸擴散框架，通過基於輸入圖的迭代精煉來生成文本，稱為圖的擴散語言模型（DLM4G）。DLM4G通過將圖元件（實體/關係）與其對應的序列標記對齊，採用了自適應噪聲策略。所提出的策略使用每個標記的去噪誤差作為信號，自適應地調節實體和關係標記上的噪聲，改善圖結構的保留，並在圖編輯下實現局部更新。在三個數據集上的評估中，DLM4G在表面形式和基於嵌入的指標上，始終超越在相同分割上訓練的競爭性G2S擴散基準。DLM4G進一步超越了微調的自回歸基準，後者的規模大達12倍（例如，T5-Large），並且在零樣本LLM轉移基準中與規模達127倍的模型具有競爭力。相對於最強的微調PLM基準，DLM4G在事實基礎（FGT@0.5）上提高了+5.16%，在編輯敏感性（ESR）上提高了+7.9%；與最佳擴散基準相比，它在FGT@0.5上獲得了+3.75%的增益，在ESR上獲得了+23.6%的增益。我們還通過分子標題生成的實驗展示了該方法在文本圖之外的適用性，表明該方法對於科學G2S生成的普遍性。

##### **The Pragmatic Persona: Discovering LLM Persona through Bridging Inference**
2604.24079v1 by Jisoo Yang, Jongwon Ryu, Minuk Ma, Trung X. Pham, Junyeong Kim

Large Language Models (LLMs) reveal inherent and distinctive personas through dialogue. However, most existing persona discovery approaches rely on surface-level lexical or stylistic cues, treating dialogue as a flat sequence of tokens and failing to capture the deeper discourse-level structures that sustain persona consistency. To address this limitation, we propose a novel analytical framework that interprets LLM dialogue through bridging inference -- implicit conceptual relations that connect utterances via shared world knowledge and discourse coherence. By modeling these relations as structured knowledge graphs, our approach captures latent semantic links that govern how LLMs organize meaning across turns, enabling persona discovery at the level of discourse coherence rather than surface realizations. Experimental results across multiple reasoning backbones and target LLMs, ranging from small-scale models to 80B-parameter systems, demonstrate that bridging-inference graphs yield significantly stronger semantic coherence and more stable persona identification than frequency or style-based baselines. These results show that persona traits are consistently encoded in the structural organization of discourse rather than isolated lexical patterns. This work presents a systematic framework for probing, extracting, and visualizing latent LLM personas through the lens of Cognitive Discourse Theory, bridging computational linguistics, cognitive semantics, and persona reasoning in large language models. Codes are available at https://github.com/JiSoo-Yang/Persona_Bridging.git

摘要：大型語言模型（LLMs）透過對話揭示出固有且獨特的人格特質。<lb/>然而，大多數現有的人格發現方法依賴於表面層的詞彙或風格線索，將對話視為一個平坦的符號序列，未能捕捉到維持人格一致性的更深層對話結構。<lb/>為了解決這一限制，我們提出了一個新穎的分析框架，通過橋接推理來解釋LLM對話——這是通過共享的世界知識和對話連貫性來連接發言的隱含概念關係。<lb/>通過將這些關係建模為結構化知識圖，我們的方法捕捉到潛在的語義聯繫，這些聯繫支配著LLMs如何在輪次之間組織意義，使人格發現能夠在對話連貫性層面進行，而不是表面實現層面。<lb/>在多個推理骨幹和目標LLMs上進行的實驗結果，涵蓋從小型模型到80B參數系統，顯示橋接推理圖在語義連貫性和人格識別的穩定性上顯著優於基於頻率或風格的基準。<lb/>這些結果表明，人格特徵在對話的結構組織中持續編碼，而不是孤立的詞彙模式。<lb/>這項工作提出了一個系統化的框架，通過認知對話理論的視角來探測、提取和可視化潛在的LLM人格，橋接計算語言學、認知語義學和大型語言模型中的人格推理。<lb/>代碼可在 https://github.com/JiSoo-Yang/Persona_Bridging.git 獲得。

##### **Grounding Before Generalizing: How AI Differs from Humans in Causal Transfer**
2604.24062v1 by Liangru Xiang, Yuxi Ma, Zhihao Cao, Yixin Zhu, Song-Chun Zhu

Extracting abstract causal structures and applying them to novel situations is a hallmark of human intelligence. While Large Language Models (LLMs) and Vision Language Models (VLMs) have shown strong performance on a wide range of reasoning tasks, their capacity for interactive causal learning -- inducing latent structures through sequential exploration and transferring them across contexts -- remains uncharacterized. Human learners accomplish such transfer after minimal exposure, whereas classical Reinforcement Learning (RL) agents fail catastrophically. Whether state-of-the-art Artificial Intelligence (AI) models possess human-like mechanisms for abstract causal structure transfer is an open question. Using the OpenLock paradigm requiring sequential discovery of Common Cause (CC) and Common Effect (CE) structures, here we show that models exhibit fundamentally delayed or absent transfer: even successful models require initial environmental-specific mapping -- what we term environmental grounding -- before efficiency gains emerge, whereas humans leverage prior structural knowledge from the very first solution attempt. In the text-only condition, models matched or exceeded human discovery efficiency. In contrast, visual information -- in both the image-only and text-and-image conditions -- overall degraded rather than enhanced performance, revealing a broad reliance on symbolic processing rather than integrated multimodal reasoning. Models further exhibited systematic CC/CE asymmetries absent in humans, suggesting heuristic biases rather than direction-neutral causal abstraction. These findings reveal that large-scale statistical learning does not produce the decontextualized causal schemas underpinning human analogical reasoning, establishing grounding-dependent transfer as a fundamental limitation of current LLMs and VLMs.

摘要：提取抽象因果結構並將其應用於新情境是人類智慧的一個特徵。雖然大型語言模型（LLMs）和視覺語言模型（VLMs）在各種推理任務上表現出色，但它們在互動式因果學習方面的能力——通過序列探索誘導潛在結構並在不同上下文中轉移它們——仍然未被表徵。人類學習者在最小的暴露後能夠完成這種轉移，而傳統的強化學習（RL）代理則會遭遇災難性的失敗。最先進的人工智慧（AI）模型是否具有人類類似的抽象因果結構轉移機制仍然是一個未解之謎。使用OpenLock範式，要求對共同原因（CC）和共同效果（CE）結構進行序列發現，我們在此顯示模型表現出根本性延遲或缺失的轉移：即使是成功的模型也需要最初的環境特定映射——我們稱之為環境基礎——才能出現效率增益，而人類則從第一次解決嘗試中利用先前的結構知識。在僅有文本的條件下，模型的發現效率與人類相當或超過。相比之下，視覺信息——在僅有圖像和文本與圖像的條件下——整體上降低了而不是提升了性能，顯示出對符號處理的廣泛依賴，而不是綜合的多模態推理。模型還表現出系統性的CC/CE不對稱，而人類則不存在這種情況，這表明存在啟發式偏見，而不是方向中立的因果抽象。這些發現揭示了大規模統計學習並未產生支撐人類類比推理的去情境化因果模式，確立了依賴基礎的轉移作為當前LLMs和VLMs的一個基本限制。

##### **From Skill Text to Skill Structure: The Scheduling-Structural-Logical Representation for Agent Skills**
2604.24026v2 by Qiliang Liang, Hansi Wang, Zhong Liang, Yang Liu

LLM agents increasingly rely on reusable skills, capability packages that combine instructions, control flow, constraints, and tool calls. In most current agent systems, however, skills are still represented by text-heavy artifacts, including SKILL{.}md-style documents and structured records whose machine-usable evidence remains embedded largely in natural-language descriptions. This poses a challenge for skill-centered agent systems: managing skill collections and using skills to support agent both require reasoning over invocation interfaces, execution structure, and concrete side effects that are often entangled in a single textual surface. An explicit representation of skill knowledge may therefore help make these artifacts easier for machines to acquire and leverage. Drawing on Memory Organization Packets, Script Theory, and Conceptual Dependency from Schank and Abelson's classical work on linguistic knowledge representation, we introduce what is, to our knowledge, the first structured representation for agent skill artifacts that disentangles skill-level scheduling signals, scene-level execution structure, and logic-level action and resource-use evidence: the Scheduling-Structural-Logical (SSL) representation. We instantiate SSL with an LLM-based normalizer and evaluate it on a corpus of skills in two tasks, Skill Discovery and Risk Assessment, and superiorly outperform the text-only baselines: in Skill Discovery, SSL improves MRR from 0.573 to 0.707; in Risk Assessment, it improves macro F1 from 0.744 to 0.787. These findings reveal that explicit, source-grounded structure makes agent skills easier to search and review. They also suggest that SSL is best understood as a practical step toward more inspectable, reusable, and operationally actionable skill representations for agent systems, rather than as a finished standard or an end-to-end mechanism for managing and using skills.

摘要：LLM 代理越來越依賴可重用的技能，這些技能包結合了指令、控制流程、約束和工具調用。然而，在大多數當前的代理系統中，技能仍然以文本為主的工件來表示，包括 SKILL{.}md 風格的文檔和結構化記錄，其機器可用的證據仍然主要嵌入在自然語言描述中。這對以技能為中心的代理系統提出了挑戰：管理技能集合和使用技能來支持代理都需要對調用介面、執行結構和具體副作用進行推理，而這些通常糾纏在單一的文本表面中。因此，技能知識的明確表示可能有助於使這些工件更容易被機器獲取和利用。基於記憶組織包、腳本理論以及 Schank 和 Abelson 在語言知識表示方面的經典工作中的概念依賴，我們介紹了我們所知的第一個結構化表示，用於代理技能工件，該表示解開了技能級調度信號、場景級執行結構和邏輯級行動及資源使用證據：調度-結構-邏輯 (SSL) 表示。我們用基於 LLM 的標準化器實現了 SSL，並在兩個任務的技能語料庫上進行評估，分別是技能發現和風險評估，並在性能上優於僅文本基準：在技能發現中，SSL 將 MRR 從 0.573 提高到 0.707；在風險評估中，將宏觀 F1 從 0.744 提高到 0.787。這些發現揭示了明確的、基於來源的結構使代理技能更容易搜索和審查。它們還表明，SSL 最好被理解為朝向更可檢查、可重用和可操作的技能表示的實際一步，而不是作為一個完成的標準或端到端的機制來管理和使用技能。

##### **Propagation Structure-Semantic Transfer Learning for Robust Fake News Detection**
2604.23974v1 by Mengyang Chen, Lingwei Wei, Han Cao, Wei Zhou, Zhou Yan, Songlin Hu

Fake news generally refers to false information that is spread deliberately to deceive people, which has detrimental social effects. Existing fake news detection methods primarily learn the semantic features from news content or integrate structural features from propagation. However, in practical scenarios, due to the semantic ambiguity of informal language and unreliable user interactive behaviors on social media, there are inherent semantic and structural noises in news content and propagation. Although some recent works consider the effect of irrelevant user interactions in a hybrid-modeling way, they still suffer from the mutual interference between structural noise and semantic noise, leading to limited performance for robust detection. To alleviate this issue, this paper proposes a novel Propagation Structure-Semantic Transfer Learning framework (PSS-TL) for robust fake news detection under a teacher-student architecture. Specifically, we design dual teacher models to learn semantics knowledge and structure knowledge from noisy news content and propagation structure independently. Besides, we design a Multi-channel Knowledge Distillation (MKD) loss to enable the student model to acquire specialized knowledge from the teacher models, thereby avoiding mutual interference. Extensive experiments on two real-world datasets validate the effectiveness and robustness of our method.

摘要：假新聞通常指的是故意散播的虛假信息，以欺騙人們，這對社會造成了有害的影響。現有的假新聞檢測方法主要從新聞內容中學習語義特徵或整合來自傳播的結構特徵。然而，在實際場景中，由於非正式語言的語義模糊性和社交媒體上不可靠的用戶互動行為，新聞內容和傳播中存在固有的語義和結構噪聲。儘管一些近期的研究以混合建模的方式考慮了無關用戶互動的影響，但它們仍然受到結構噪聲和語義噪聲之間的相互干擾，導致穩健檢測的性能有限。為了緩解這一問題，本文提出了一種新穎的傳播結構-語義轉移學習框架（PSS-TL），用於在教師-學生架構下進行穩健的假新聞檢測。具體而言，我們設計了雙教師模型，獨立地從噪聲新聞內容和傳播結構中學習語義知識和結構知識。此外，我們設計了一種多通道知識蒸餾（MKD）損失，以使學生模型能夠從教師模型中獲取專門知識，從而避免相互干擾。在兩個真實世界數據集上的大量實驗驗證了我們方法的有效性和穩健性。

##### **Quantum Knowledge Graph: Modeling Context-Dependent Triplet Validity**
2604.23972v1 by Yao Wang, Zixu Geng, Jun Yan

Knowledge graphs (KGs) are increasingly used to support large lan guage model (LLM) reasoning, but standard triplet-based KGs treat each relation as globally valid. In many settings, whether a relation should count as evidence depends on the context. We therefore formulate triplet validity as a triplet-specific function of context and refer to this formulation as a Quantum Knowledge Graph (QKG). We instantiate QKG in medicine using a diabetes-centered PrimeKG subgraph, whose 68,651 context-sensitive relations are further annotated with patient-group-specific constraints. We evaluate it in a reasoner--validator pipeline for medical question answering on a KG-grounded subset of MedReason containing 2,788 questions. With Haiku-4.5 as both the Reasoner and the Validator, KG-backed validation significantly improves over a no-validator baseline ($+0.61$ pp), and QKG with context matching yields the largest gain, outperforming both KG validation without context matching ($+0.79$ pp) and the no-validator baseline ($+1.40$ pp; paired McNemar, all $p<0.05$). Under a stronger validator (Qwen-3.6-Plus), the raw QKG gain over the no-validator baseline grows from $+1.40$ pp to $+5.96$ pp; the context-matching gap is non-significant ($p=0.73$) on the raw set but becomes borderline significant ($p=0.05$) after adjustment for knowledge leakage and suspicious questions, consistent with a benchmark-gold ceiling rather than a QKG limitation. Taken together, the results support the view that the value of a KG in LLM-based clinical reasoning lies not merely in storing medically related facts, but in representing whether those facts are applicable to the specific patient context. For reproducibility and further research, we release the curated QKG datasets and source code.\footnote{https://github.com/HKAI-Sci/QKG}

摘要：知識圖譜（KGs）越來越多地用於支持大型語言模型（LLM）的推理，但標準的基於三元組的KGs將每個關係視為全局有效。在許多情境中，某個關係是否應該被視為證據取決於上下文。因此，我們將三元組的有效性表述為一個特定於三元組的上下文函數，並將這一表述稱為量子知識圖譜（QKG）。我們在醫學中實現QKG，使用以糖尿病為中心的PrimeKG子圖，其68,651個上下文敏感的關係進一步附加了特定於患者群體的約束。我們在一個推理者-驗證者管道中對其進行評估，針對KG基礎的MedReason子集進行醫學問題回答，該子集包含2,788個問題。使用Haiku-4.5作為推理者和驗證者，KG支持的驗證顯著改善了無驗證者基線（$+0.61$ pp），而具有上下文匹配的QKG則產生了最大的增益，超越了沒有上下文匹配的KG驗證（$+0.79$ pp）和無驗證者基線（$+1.40$ pp；配對McNemar，所有$p&lt;0.05$）。在一個更強的驗證者（Qwen-3.6-Plus）下，原始QKG相對於無驗證者基線的增益從$+1.40$ pp增長到$+5.96$ pp；在原始數據集上，上下文匹配的差距不顯著（$p=0.73$），但在調整知識洩露和可疑問題後變得邊際顯著（$p=0.05$），這與基準金標準上限一致，而不是QKG的限制。綜合來看，結果支持這樣的觀點：KG在基於LLM的臨床推理中的價值不僅在於存儲醫學相關事實，還在於表示這些事實是否適用於特定的患者上下文。為了可重複性和進一步研究，我們釋放了經過策劃的QKG數據集和源代碼。\footnote{https://github.com/HKAI-Sci/QKG}

##### **LLM-Guided Agentic Floor Plan Parsing for Accessible Indoor Navigation of Blind and Low-Vision People**
2604.23970v1 by Aydin Ayanzadeh, Tim Oates

Indoor navigation remains a critical accessibility challenge for the blind and low-vision (BLV) individuals, as existing solutions rely on costly per-building infrastructure. We present an agentic framework that converts a single floor plan image into a structured, retrievable knowledge base to generate safe, accessible navigation instructions with lightweight infrastructure. The system has two phases: a multi-agent module that parses the floor plan into a spatial knowledge graph through a self-correcting pipeline with iterative retry loops and corrective feedback; and a Path Planner that generates accessible navigation instructions, with a Safety Evaluator agent assessing potential hazards along each route. We evaluate the system on the real-world UMBC Math and Psychology building (floors MP-1 and MP-3) and on the CVC-FP benchmark. On MP-1, we achieve success rates of 92.31%, 76.92%, and 61.54% for short, medium, and long routes, outperforming the strongest single-call baseline (Claude 3.7 Sonnet) at 84.62%, 69.23%, and 53.85%. On MP-3, we reach 76.92%, 61.54%, and 38.46%, compared to the best baseline at 61.54%, 46.15%, and 23.08%. These results show consistent gains over single-call LLM baselines and demonstrate that our workflow is a scalable solution for accessible indoor navigation for BLV individuals.

摘要：室內導航對盲人和低視力（BLV）個體來說仍然是一個關鍵的可及性挑戰，因為現有的解決方案依賴於昂貴的每棟建築基礎設施。<lb/>我們提出了一個代理框架，將單一樓層平面圖像轉換為結構化的可檢索知識庫，以生成安全、可及的導航指示，並使用輕量級基礎設施。<lb/>該系統有兩個階段：一個多代理模塊，通過自我校正的管道和迭代重試循環及校正反饋，將樓層平面圖解析為空間知識圖；以及一個路徑規劃器，生成可及的導航指示，並由安全評估代理評估每條路徑上的潛在危險。<lb/>我們在現實世界的UMBC數學與心理學大樓（MP-1和MP-3樓層）以及CVC-FP基準上評估該系統。<lb/>在MP-1上，我們的成功率分別為92.31%、76.92%和61.54%，對於短、中和長路徑，超越了最強的單次調用基線（Claude 3.7 Sonnet）的84.62%、69.23%和53.85%。<lb/>在MP-3上，我們達到76.92%、61.54%和38.46%，相比之下最佳基線為61.54%、46.15%和23.08%。<lb/>這些結果顯示出相對於單次調用LLM基線的一致增長，並證明我們的工作流程是為BLV個體提供可及室內導航的可擴展解決方案。

##### **GamED.AI: A Hierarchical Multi-Agent Framework for Automated Educational Game Generation**
2604.23947v2 by Shiven Agarwal, Yash Shah, Ashish Raj Shekhar, Priyanuj Bordoloi, Vivek Gupta

We introduce GamED.AI, a hierarchical multi-agent framework that transforms instructor-provided questions into fully playable, pedagogically grounded educational games validated through formal mechanic contracts. Built on phase-based LangGraph sub-graphs, deterministic Quality Gates, and structured Pydantic schemas, GamED.AI supports two template families encompassing 15 interaction mechanics across spatial reasoning, procedural execution, and higher-order Bloom's Taxonomy objectives. Evaluated on 200 questions spanning five subject domains, the system achieves a 90% validation pass rate, 98.3% schema compliance, and 73% token reduction over ReAct agents (${\sim}$73,500 $\rightarrow$ ${\sim}$19,900 tokens/game) at $0.46 per game. Within this model configuration, these results suggest that phase-bounded architectural structure correlates more strongly with alignment quality than prompting strategy alone. Our demonstration lets attendees generate Bloom's-aligned games from natural language in under 60 seconds, inspect Quality Gate outputs at each pipeline phase, and browse a curated library of 50 games spanning all 15 mechanic types.

摘要：我們介紹 GamED.AI，一個層級多代理框架，將講師提供的問題轉換為完全可玩、以教學為基礎的教育遊戲，並通過正式的機械合約進行驗證。該框架基於基於階段的 LangGraph 子圖、確定性的質量門和結構化的 Pydantic 模式，GamED.AI 支持兩個模板系列，涵蓋 15 種互動機制，涉及空間推理、程序執行和高階布魯姆分類法目標。在涵蓋五個學科領域的 200 個問題上進行評估，該系統實現了 90% 的驗證通過率、98.3% 的模式合規性，以及相較於 ReAct 代理的 73% 令牌減少（${\sim}$73,500 $\rightarrow$ ${\sim}$19,900 tokens/game），每個遊戲的成本為 $0.46。在這種模型配置中，這些結果表明，階段限制的架構結構與對齊質量的相關性比單純的提示策略更強。我們的演示讓參與者在 60 秒內從自然語言生成與布魯姆對齊的遊戲，檢查每個管道階段的質量門輸出，並瀏覽涵蓋所有 15 種機制類型的 50 款遊戲的策展庫。

##### **Agentic AI platforms for autonomous training and rule induction of human-human and virus-human protein-protein interactions**
2604.23924v1 by Hung N. Do, Jessica Z. Kubicek-Sutherland, Oscar A. Negrete, S. Gnanakaran

We instruct an AI agent to construct two separate agentic AI platforms: one for autonomous training of predictive ML models for human-human and virus-human PPI, and the other for inducing explicit general rules governing human-human and virus-human PPI. The first agentic AI platform for autonomous training of predictive ML models for PPI is designed to consist of five AI agents that handle autonomous data collection, data verification, feature embedding, model design, and training and validation on three-way protein-disjoint cross-fold datasets. For human-human and human-virus PPIs, the final three-way protein-disjoint ensemble achieves an accuracy of 87.3% and 86.5%, respectively. For cross-checking and interpretability purposes, the second agentic AI platform is designed to replace ML predictions with human-readable rules derived from protein embeddings, physicochemical autocovariance descriptors, compartment annotations, pathway-domain overlap, and graph contexts. For human-human PPI, it is defined by a two-rule induction, whereas human-virus is induced by a more complex set of weighted rules. The rules induced by the second agentic platform align with the SHAP-identified features from the predictive ML models built by the first agentic platform. Taken together, our work demonstrates the agentic AI's ability to orchestrate from data planning to execution, and from rule induction to explanation in ML, opening the door to various applications.

摘要：我們指示一個 AI 代理構建兩個獨立的代理 AI 平台：一個用於自主訓練人類-人類和病毒-人類 PPI 的預測 ML 模型，另一個用於引導明確的通用規則，規範人類-人類和病毒-人類 PPI。第一個用於自主訓練 PPI 預測 ML 模型的代理 AI 平台設計為由五個 AI 代理組成，這些代理負責自主數據收集、數據驗證、特徵嵌入、模型設計，以及在三向蛋白質不重疊交叉折疊數據集上的訓練和驗證。對於人類-人類和人類-病毒 PPI，最終的三向蛋白質不重疊集成模型分別達到了 87.3% 和 86.5% 的準確率。為了進行交叉檢查和可解釋性目的，第二個代理 AI 平台設計為用從蛋白質嵌入、物理化學自協方差描述符、區域註釋、途徑-領域重疊和圖形上下文中派生的人類可讀規則來替代 ML 預測。對於人類-人類 PPI，它由兩條規則引導，而人類-病毒則由一組更複雜的加權規則引導。第二個代理平台引導的規則與第一個代理平台構建的預測 ML 模型中的 SHAP 識別特徵相一致。總的來說，我們的工作展示了代理 AI 從數據規劃到執行，從規則引導到 ML 解釋的能力，為各種應用開啟了大門。

##### **Knowledge Vector of Logical Reasoning in Large Language Models**
2604.23877v1 by Zixuan Wang, Yuanyuan Lei

Logical reasoning serve as a central capability in LLMs and includes three main forms: deductive, inductive, and abductive reasoning. In this work, we study the knowledge representations of these reasoning types in LLMs and analyze the correlations among them. Our analysis shows that each form of logical reasoning can be captured as a reasoning-specific knowledge vector in a linear representation space, yet these vectors are largely independent of each other. Motivated by cognitive science theory that these subforms of logical reasoning interact closely in the human brain, as well as our observation that the reasoning process for one type can benefit from the reasoning chain produced by another, we further propose to refine the knowledge representations of each reasoning type in LLMs to encourage complementarity between them. To this end, we design a complementary subspace-constrained refinement framework, which introduces a complementary loss that enables each reasoning vector to leverage auxiliary knowledge from the others, and a subspace constraint loss that prevents erasure of their unique characteristics. Through steering experiments along reasoning vectors, we find that refined vectors incorporating complementary knowledge yield consistent performance gains. We also conduct a mechanism-interpretability analysis of each reasoning vector, revealing insights into the shared and specific features of different reasoning in LLMs.

摘要：邏輯推理作為大型語言模型（LLMs）的核心能力，包括三種主要形式：演繹推理、歸納推理和溯因推理。<lb/>在本研究中，我們研究這些推理類型在LLMs中的知識表示，並分析它們之間的相關性。<lb/>我們的分析顯示，每種邏輯推理形式都可以在線性表示空間中被捕捉為特定於推理的知識向量，但這些向量彼此之間大體上是獨立的。<lb/>受到認知科學理論的啟發，這些邏輯推理的子形式在人的大腦中密切互動，以及我們觀察到一種類型的推理過程可以受益於另一種類型產生的推理鏈，我們進一步提出在LLMs中細化每種類型的知識表示，以促進它們之間的互補性。<lb/>為此，我們設計了一個互補子空間約束的細化框架，該框架引入了一種互補損失，使每個推理向量能夠利用來自其他向量的輔助知識，並引入一種子空間約束損失，以防止其獨特特徵的消失。<lb/>通過沿著推理向量進行引導實驗，我們發現 incorporating 互補知識的細化向量產生了一致的性能提升。<lb/>我們還對每個推理向量進行了機制可解釋性分析，揭示了LLMs中不同推理的共享和特定特徵的見解。

##### **Graph Memory Transformer (GMT)**
2604.23862v1 by Nicola Zanarini, Niccolò Ferrari

We investigate whether the Feed-Forward Network (FFN) sublayer in a decoder-only transformer can be replaced by an explicit learned memory graph while preserving the surrounding autoregressive architecture. The proposed Graph Memory Transformer (GMT) keeps causal self-attention intact, but replaces the usual per-token FFN transformation with a memory cell that routes token representations over a learned bank of centroids connected by a learned directed transition matrix. In the base GMT v7 instantiation studied here, each of 16 transformer blocks contains 128 centroids, a 128 * 128 edge matrix, gravitational source routing, token-conditioned target selection, and a gated displacement readout. The cell therefore returns movement from an estimated source memory state toward a target memory state, rather than a retrieved value. The resulting model is a fully decoder-only language model with 82.2M trainable parameters and no dense FFN sublayers, compared with a 103.0M-parameter dense GPT-style baseline used in the evaluation. The base v7 model trains stably and exposes centroid usage, transition structure, and source-to-target movement as directly inspectable quantities of the forward computation. It remains behind the larger dense baseline in validation loss and perplexity (3.5995/36.58 vs. 3.2903/26.85), while showing close zero-shot benchmark behavior under the evaluated setting. These results are not intended as a state-of-the-art claim; they support the viability and structural interpretability of replacing dense within-token transformation with graph-mediated memory navigation. Broader scaling, optimized kernels, and more extensive benchmark evaluation are left for subsequent work.

摘要：我們調查了在僅解碼器的Transformer中，前饋網絡（FFN）子層是否可以被明確學習的記憶圖所取代，同時保持周圍的自回歸架構。所提出的圖記憶Transformer（GMT）保持因果自注意力不變，但用一個記憶單元取代了通常的每個標記的FFN變換，該記憶單元通過一個學習的有向轉移矩陣將標記表示路由到一個學習的質心庫。這裡研究的基礎GMT v7實例中，每個16個Transformer塊包含128個質心、一個128 * 128的邊緣矩陣、重力源路由、標記條件目標選擇和一個門控位移讀出。因此，該單元返回從估計的源記憶狀態向目標記憶狀態的運動，而不是檢索的值。與在評估中使用的103.0M參數的密集GPT風格基線相比，所得到的模型是一個完全的僅解碼器語言模型，擁有82.2M可訓練參數，且沒有密集的FFN子層。基礎v7模型穩定訓練，並將質心使用、轉移結構和源到目標的運動暴露為可直接檢查的前向計算量。它在驗證損失和困惑度上仍落後於更大的密集基線（3.5995/36.58對比3.2903/26.85），同時在評估設置下顯示出接近零樣本基準行為。這些結果並不旨在作為最先進的聲明；它們支持用圖介導的記憶導航取代密集的內部標記變換的可行性和結構可解釋性。更廣泛的擴展、優化內核和更廣泛的基準評估將留待後續工作。

##### **Scalable Production Scheduling: Linear Complexity via Unified Homogeneous Graphs**
2604.23841v1 by Jonathan Hoss, Moritz Link, Noah Klarmann

Efficiently solving the Job Shop Scheduling Problem in real-world industrial applications requires policies that are both computationally lean and topologically robust. While Reinforcement Learning has shown potential in automating dispatching rules, existing models often struggle with a scalability bottleneck caused by quadratic graph complexity or the architectural overhead of heterogeneous layers. We introduce a unified graph framework that employs feature-based homogenization to project distinct node roles into a shared latent space. This allows a standard homogeneous Graph Isomorphism Network to capture complex resource contention with linear complexity, ensuring low-latency inference for large-scale industrial applications. Our empirical results demonstrate that our framework achieves state-of-the-art performance while exhibiting consistent zero-shot generalization. We identify the job-to-machine ratio as the primary driver of policy effectiveness, rather than absolute problem size. Based on this, we propose a hypothesis of structural saturation, demonstrating that policies trained on critically congested instances ($\mathcal{J} \approx \mathcal{M}$) learn scale-invariant resolution strategies. Agents trained at this saturation point internalize invariant conflict-resolution logic, allowing them to treat massive rectangular instances as a sequential concatenation of saturated sub-problems. This approach eliminates the need for expensive scale-specific retraining and prevents overfitting to statistical shortcuts, providing a robust and efficient pathway for deploying RL solutions in dynamic production environments.

摘要：有效解決實際工業應用中的工作車間排程問題需要既計算高效又拓撲穩健的政策。雖然強化學習在自動化調度規則方面顯示出潛力，但現有模型往往面臨由於二次圖形複雜性或異構層的架構開銷造成的可擴展性瓶頸。我們提出了一個統一的圖形框架，利用基於特徵的同質化將不同的節點角色投影到共享的潛在空間。這使得標準的同質圖同構網絡能以線性複雜度捕捉複雜的資源競爭，確保在大規模工業應用中進行低延遲推斷。我們的實證結果表明，我們的框架實現了最先進的性能，同時展現出一致的零樣本泛化。我們確定工作與機器的比例是政策有效性的主要驅動因素，而不是絕對問題大小。基於此，我們提出了一個結構飽和的假設，證明在臨界擁擠實例上訓練的政策（$\mathcal{J} \approx \mathcal{M}$）學會了尺度不變的解決策略。在這個飽和點訓練的代理內化了不變的衝突解決邏輯，使他們能將大規模矩形實例視為飽和子問題的序列串聯。這種方法消除了對昂貴的特定規模再訓練的需求，並防止了對統計捷徑的過擬合，為在動態生產環境中部署強化學習解決方案提供了一條穩健而高效的途徑。

##### **Domain-Filtered Knowledge Graphs from Sparse Autoencoder Features**
2604.23829v2 by John Winnicki, Abeynaya Gnanasekaran, Eric Darve

Sparse autoencoders (SAEs) extract millions of interpretable features from a language model, but flat feature inventories aren't very useful on their own. Domain concepts get mixed with generic and weakly grounded features, while related ideas are scattered across many units, and there's no way to understand relationships between features. We address this by first constructing a strict domain-specific concept universe from a large SAE inventory using contrastive activations and a multi-stage filtering process. Next, we build two aligned graph views on the filtered set: a co-occurrence graph for corpus-level conceptual structure, organized at multiple levels of granularity, and a transcoder-based mechanism graph that links source-layer and target-layer features through sparse latent pathways. Automated edge labeling then turns these graph views into readable knowledge graphs rather than unlabeled layouts. In a case study on a biology textbook, these graphs recover coherent chapter and subchapter-level structure, reveal concepts that bridge neighboring topics, and transform messy sentence-level activity containing thousands of features into compact, readable views that illustrate the model's local activity. Taken together, this reframes a flat SAE inventory as an internal knowledge graph that converts feature-level interpretability into a global map of model knowledge and enables audits of reasoning faithfulness.

摘要：稀疏自編碼器（SAEs）從語言模型中提取數百萬個可解釋的特徵，但平坦的特徵庫本身並不太有用。領域概念與一般性和弱基礎的特徵混合在一起，而相關的想法則散布在許多單元中，沒有辦法理解特徵之間的關係。我們通過首先使用對比激活和多階段過濾過程，從大型SAE庫構建一個嚴格的領域特定概念宇宙來解決這個問題。接下來，我們在過濾後的集合上構建兩個對齊的圖視圖：一個用於語料庫級概念結構的共現圖，按多個粒度級別組織，以及一個基於轉碼器的機制圖，通過稀疏潛在通道將源層和目標層特徵連接起來。自動邊緣標籤化隨後將這些圖視圖轉換為可讀的知識圖，而不是未標記的佈局。在一項針對生物學教科書的案例研究中，這些圖恢復了連貫的章節和子章節級結構，揭示了橋接相鄰主題的概念，並將包含數千個特徵的雜亂句子級活動轉換為緊湊、可讀的視圖，展示模型的局部活動。綜合來看，這將平坦的SAE庫重新構架為一個內部知識圖，將特徵級的可解釋性轉換為模型知識的全球地圖，並使推理的忠實性審計成為可能。

##### **Domain Fine-Tuning vs. Retrieval-Augmented Generation for Medical Multiple-Choice Question Answering: A Controlled Comparison at the 4B-Parameter Scale**
2604.23801v1 by Avi-ad Avraam Buskila

Practitioners deploying small open-weight large language models (LLMs) for medical question answering face a recurring design choice: invest in a domain-fine-tuned model, or keep a general-purpose model and inject domain knowledge at inference time via retrieval-augmented generation (RAG). We isolate this trade-off by holding model size, prompt template, decoding temperature, retrieval pipeline, and evaluation protocol fixed, and varying only (i) whether the model has been domain-adapted (Gemma 3 4B vs. MedGemma 4B, both 4-bit quantized and served via Ollama) and (ii) whether retrieved passages from a medical knowledge corpus are inserted into the prompt. We evaluate all four cells of this 2x2 design on the full MedQA-USMLE 4-option test split (1,273 questions) with three repetitions per question (15,276 LLM calls). Domain fine-tuning yields a +6.8 percentage-point gain in majority-vote accuracy over the general 4B baseline (53.3% vs. 46.4%, McNemar p < 10^-4). RAG over MedMCQA explanations does not produce a statistically significant gain in either model, and in the domain-tuned model the point estimate is slightly negative (-1.9 pp, p = 0.16). At this scale and on this benchmark, domain knowledge encoded in weights dominates domain knowledge supplied in context. We release the full experiment code and JSONL traces to support replication.

摘要：從事小型開放權重大型語言模型（LLMs）用於醫學問題回答的實踐者面臨一個反覆出現的設計選擇：投資於一個領域微調的模型，還是保留一個通用模型並在推理時通過檢索增強生成（RAG）注入領域知識。<lb/>我們通過固定模型大小、提示模板、解碼溫度、檢索管道和評估協議，並僅變化（i）模型是否經過領域適應（Gemma 3 4B 與 MedGemma 4B，均為 4 位元量化並通過 Ollama 提供服務）以及（ii）是否將來自醫學知識語料庫的檢索段落插入提示中，來隔離這一權衡。<lb/>我們在完整的 MedQA-USMLE 4 選項測試拆分（1,273 個問題）上評估這個 2x2 設計的四個單元，每個問題重複三次（15,276 次 LLM 調用）。<lb/>領域微調相對於一般的 4B 基線（53.3% 對 46.4%，McNemar p < 10^-4）帶來了 +6.8 個百分點的多數投票準確率增益。<lb/>在兩個模型中，對 MedMCQA 解釋的 RAG 並未產生統計上顯著的增益，而在領域微調的模型中，點估計略為負值（-1.9 pp，p = 0.16）。<lb/>在這個規模和這個基準下，編碼在權重中的領域知識主導了在上下文中提供的領域知識。<lb/>我們發布完整的實驗代碼和 JSONL 跟蹤，以支持重複實驗。

##### **The Override Gap: A Magnitude Account of Knowledge Conflict Failure in Hypernetwork-Based Instant LLM Adaptation**
2604.23750v1 by Shuaizhi Cheng, Xiang Shi, Mingwei Li

Hypernetwork-based methods such as Doc-to-LoRA internalize a document into an LLM's weights in a single forward pass, but they fail systematically on conflicts: when the document contradicts pretraining knowledge, accuracy collapses to 46.4% on the deepest facts. We show the failure is a magnitude problem rather than a representational one. The hypernetwork already targets the right layers, but its adapter margin is approximately constant across documents while the pretrained margin grows with training frequency, so deep conflicts lose by construction. The account predicts that failure should track prior strength: sorting 194 conflicts by the base model's log-probability on the contradicted fact, baseline accuracy falls from 68% on weak-prior questions to 16% on strong-prior ones, a 52 percentage-point gap. The cure is amplitude. Selective Layer Boosting scales the adapter at its top-norm layers, and Conflict-Aware Internalization triggers boosting only when the base model is confident. Both are training-free; together they raise deep-conflict accuracy from 46.4% to 71.0% on Gemma-2B and from 53.6% to 72.5% on Mistral-7B while preserving novel-knowledge recall, and beat vanilla retrieval-augmented generation on medium conflicts by 18 percentage points despite operating entirely in parameter space. We release KID-Bench, a 489-question benchmark that separates novel recall, cross-knowledge combination, and prior-graded conflicts.

摘要：基於超網絡的方法，如 Doc-to-LoRA，將文檔內化到 LLM 的權重中，僅需一次前向傳遞，但在衝突上系統性失敗：當文檔與預訓練知識相矛盾時，對於最深的事實，準確率降至 46.4%。我們顯示這一失敗是幅度問題，而非表徵問題。超網絡已經針對正確的層，但其適配器邊際在不同文檔之間大致保持不變，而預訓練邊際隨著訓練頻率的增長而增長，因此深層衝突在結構上會失敗。該解釋預測失敗應該與先前的強度相關：根據基礎模型在被矛盾事實上的對數概率對 194 個衝突進行排序，基準準確率從弱先驗問題的 68% 降至強先驗問題的 16%，相差 52 個百分點。解決方案是幅度。選擇性層增強在其頂部規範層上擴展適配器，而衝突感知內化僅在基礎模型有信心時啟動增強。這兩者都是無需訓練的；它們共同將深層衝突的準確率從 46.4% 提升至 71.0%（Gemma-2B），並將 Mistral-7B 的準確率從 53.6% 提升至 72.5%，同時保持新知識的回憶，並在中等衝突中比原始檢索增強生成高出 18 個百分點，儘管完全在參數空間中運作。我們發布了 KID-Bench，一個包含 489 個問題的基準，區分新穎回憶、跨知識組合和先驗分級衝突。

##### **Expert Evaluation of LLM's Open-Ended Legal Reasoning on the Japanese Bar Exam Writing Task**
2604.23730v1 by Jungmin Choi, Keisuke Sakaguchi, Hiroaki Yamada

Large language models (LLMs) have shown strong performance on legal benchmarks, including multiple-choice components of bar exams. However, their capacity for generating open-ended legal reasoning in realistic scenarios remains insufficiently explored. Notably, to our best knowledge, there are no prior studies or datasets addressing this issue in the Japanese context.
  This study presents the first dataset designed to evaluate the open-ended legal reasoning performance of LLMs within the Japanese jurisdiction. The dataset is based on the writing component of the Japanese bar examination, which requires examinees to identify multiple legal issues from long narratives and to construct structured legal arguments in free text format. Our key contribution is the manual evaluation of LLMs' generated responses by legal experts, which reveals limitations and challenges in legal reasoning. Moreover, we conducted a manual analysis of hallucinations to characterize when and how the models introduce content not supported by precedent or law.
  Our real exam questions, model-generated responses, and expert evaluations reveal the milestones of current LLMs in the Japanese legal domain. Our dataset and relevant resources will be available online.

摘要：大型語言模型（LLMs）在法律基準上表現出色，包括律師考試的多選題部分。然而，它們在現實情境中生成開放式法律推理的能力仍然未被充分探索。值得注意的是，據我們所知，沒有先前的研究或數據集在日本背景下解決這個問題。<lb/>本研究提出了第一個旨在評估LLMs在日本法域內開放式法律推理表現的數據集。該數據集基於日本律師考試的寫作部分，要求考生從長篇敘述中識別多個法律問題，並以自由文本格式構建結構化法律論證。我們的主要貢獻是由法律專家對LLMs生成的回應進行手動評估，這揭示了法律推理中的局限性和挑戰。此外，我們對幻覺進行了手動分析，以描述模型何時以及如何引入不受先例或法律支持的內容。<lb/>我們的真實考試問題、模型生成的回應和專家評估揭示了當前LLMs在日本法律領域的里程碑。我們的數據集和相關資源將在線上提供。

##### **ESIA: An Energy-Based Spatiotemporal Interaction-Aware Framework for Pedestrian Intention Prediction**
2604.23728v1 by Yanping Wu, Meiting Dang, Lin Wu, Edmond S. L. Ho, Zhenghua Chen, Chongfeng Wei

Recent advances in autonomous driving have motivated research on pedestrian intention prediction, which aims to infer future crossing decisions and actions by modeling temporal dynamics, social interactions, and environmental context. However, existing studies remain constrained by oversimplified multi-agent interaction patterns, opaque reasoning logic, and a lack of global consistency in behavioral predictions, which compromise both robustness and interpretability. In this work, we propose ESIA (Energy-based Spatiotemporal Interaction-Aware framework), a novel Conditional Random Field (CRF)-based paradigm. We cast the intention prediction task as a structured prediction problem over a unified graph-based representation, treating pedestrians and the environment as spatiotemporal nodes. To characterize their distinct roles, we assign unary potentials to nodes to capture individual intentions, and pairwise potentials to edges to encode social and environmental interactions. These potentials are integrated into a unified global energy function to ensure scene-level consistency across behavioral predictions. To further constrain inference without ground-truth supervision, we introduce structural consistency terms to penalize logical contradictions. This optimization is efficiently solved via a novel Unary-Seeded Simulated Annealing (U-SSA) algorithm, which leverages high-confidence unary priors to rapidly converge to a high-quality solution. Extensive experiments on standard benchmarks demonstrate that ESIA achieves state-of-the-art performance with improved interpretability over existing methods.

摘要：最近在自動駕駛方面的進展促進了對行人意圖預測的研究，該研究旨在通過建模時間動態、社會互動和環境背景來推斷未來的過馬路決策和行動。<lb/>然而，現有研究仍受到過於簡化的多代理互動模式、不透明的推理邏輯和行為預測缺乏全局一致性的限制，這妨礙了穩健性和可解釋性。<lb/>在這項工作中，我們提出了ESIA（基於能量的時空互動感知框架），這是一種新穎的基於條件隨機場（CRF）的範式。<lb/>我們將意圖預測任務視為在統一的圖形表示上的結構化預測問題，將行人和環境視為時空節點。<lb/>為了表徵它們的不同角色，我們為節點分配一元潛力以捕捉個體意圖，並為邊緣分配成對潛力以編碼社會和環境互動。<lb/>這些潛力被整合到一個統一的全局能量函數中，以確保行為預測的場景級一致性。<lb/>為了進一步約束推斷而不需要真實標準監督，我們引入結構一致性項來懲罰邏輯矛盾。<lb/>這一優化通過一種新穎的單一種子模擬退火（U-SSA）算法高效解決，該算法利用高置信度的一元先驗快速收斂到高質量解。<lb/>在標準基準上的廣泛實驗表明，ESIA在提高可解釋性方面達到了現有方法的最先進性能。

##### **An AI-Based Supervisory Measurement Integrity Validation Layer for Cyber-Resilient AC/DC Protection in Inverter-Based Microgrids**
2604.23666v1 by Ahmad Mohammad Saber, Ahmed Saber Refae, Davor Svetinovic, Hatem Zeineldin, Amr Youssef, Ehab F. El-Saadany, Deepa Kundur

Line current differential relays (LCDRs) are measurement-driven relays that rely on time-synchronized multi-phase current waveforms to infer internal faults in AC and DC power networks. In inverter-based microgrids, however, the increasing reliance on digitally communicated measurements exposes LCDRs to false-data injection attacks (FDIAs), in which adversaries manipulate remote measurement streams to create protection-triggering yet physically inconsistent current trajectories. This paper addresses this emerging measurement integrity problem by introducing a measurement integrity validation scheme that operates as a supervisory instrumentation layer for modern LCDRs. The proposed scheme interprets short windows of synchronized instantaneous current measurements recorded during relay operation and assesses their physical consistency to distinguish genuine fault-induced trajectories from cyber-manipulated measurement streams. A recurrent neural network is trained offline using only relay-available current measurements and exploits the temporal structure of differential current waveforms, which remains informative in inverter-dominated systems where current magnitude is no longer a reliable observable. The method requires no additional sensors, auxiliary protection elements, or prior knowledge of network topology, and is applicable to both AC and DC LCDRs without structural modification. The proposed measurement validation scheme is evaluated on an islanded inverter-based microgrid under a comprehensive set of fault and FDIA scenarios, demonstrating high detection accuracy while preserving relay dependability. Hardware-in-the-loop validation using an OPAL-RT real-time simulator confirms that the scheme satisfies protection timing constraints and can operate in real time under realistic operating conditions.

摘要：線電流差動繼電器（LCDRs）是基於測量的繼電器，依賴於時間同步的多相電流波形來推斷交流和直流電力網絡中的內部故障。<lb/>然而，在基於逆變器的微電網中，對數位通信測量的日益依賴使LCDRs暴露於虛假數據注入攻擊（FDIAs），在這種攻擊中，對手操縱遠程測量流，以創造觸發保護但在物理上不一致的電流軌跡。<lb/>本文針對這一新興的測量完整性問題，提出了一種測量完整性驗證方案，該方案作為現代LCDRs的監控儀器層運行。<lb/>所提出的方案解釋了在繼電器運行期間記錄的同步瞬時電流測量的短時間窗口，並評估其物理一致性，以區分真正的故障引起的軌跡與網絡操縱的測量流。<lb/>一個 recurrent neural network 在離線情況下僅使用繼電器可用的電流測量進行訓練，並利用差動電流波形的時間結構，這在電流幅度不再是可靠可觀測量的逆變器主導系統中仍然具有信息價值。<lb/>該方法不需要額外的傳感器、輔助保護元件或網絡拓撲的先驗知識，並且適用於交流和直流LCDRs，無需結構修改。<lb/>所提出的測量驗證方案在一個孤立的基於逆變器的微電網上進行評估，涵蓋了一系列故障和FDIA場景，顯示出高檢測準確率，同時保持繼電器的可靠性。<lb/>使用OPAL-RT實時模擬器進行的硬體在迴路驗證確認該方案滿足保護時間約束，並能在現實操作條件下實時運行。

##### **Structural Enforcement of Goal Integrity in AI Agents via Separation-of-Powers Architecture**
2604.23646v1 by Rong Xiang

Recent evidence suggests that frontier AI systems can exhibit agentic misalignment, generating and executing harmful actions derived from internally constructed goals, even without explicit user requests. Existing mitigation methods, such as Reinforcement Learning from Human Feedback (RLHF) and constitutional prompting, operate primarily at the model level and provide only probabilistic safety guarantees. We propose the Policy-Execution-Authorization (PEA) architecture, a "separation-of-powers" design that enforces safety at the system level. PEA decouples intent generation, authorization, and execution into independent, isolated layers connected via cryptographically constrained capability tokens. We present five core contributions: (C1) an Intent Verification Layer (IVL) for ensuring capability-intent consistency; (C2) Intent Lineage Tracking (ILT), which binds all executable intents to the originating user request via cryptographic anchors; (C3) Goal Drift Detection, which rejects semantically divergent intents below a configurable threshold; (C4) an Output Semantic Gate (OSG) that detects implicit coercion using a structured $K \times I \times P$ threat calculus (Knowledge, Influence, Policy); and (C5) a formal verification framework proving that goal integrity is maintained even under adversarial model compromise. By shifting agent alignment from a behavioral property to a structurally enforced system constraint, PEA provides a robust foundation for the governance of autonomous agents.

摘要：最近的證據表明，前沿 AI 系統可能會出現代理不一致，產生和執行源自內部構建目標的有害行為，即使沒有明確的用戶請求。現有的緩解方法，如來自人類反饋的強化學習 (RLHF) 和憲法提示，主要在模型層面運作，僅提供概率性的安全保證。我們提出了政策執行授權 (PEA) 架構，這是一種“權力分立”的設計，強制在系統層面上確保安全。PEA 將意圖生成、授權和執行解耦為獨立的、隔離的層，通過加密約束的能力令牌相連。我們提出了五個核心貢獻：(C1) 意圖驗證層 (IVL)，用於確保能力與意圖的一致性；(C2) 意圖來源追蹤 (ILT)，通過加密錨將所有可執行意圖綁定到原始用戶請求；(C3) 目標漂移檢測，拒絕低於可配置閾值的語義上不同的意圖；(C4) 輸出語義閘 (OSG)，使用結構化的 $K \times I \times P$ 威脅計算 (知識、影響、政策) 檢測隱性脅迫；以及 (C5) 一個形式驗證框架，證明即使在對抗模型妥協的情況下，目標完整性仍然得以維持。通過將代理對齊從行為屬性轉變為結構性強制的系統約束，PEA 為自主代理的治理提供了一個穩健的基礎。

##### **RaV-IDP: A Reconstruction-as-Validation Framework for Faithful Intelligent Document Processing**
2604.23644v1 by Pritesh Jha

Intelligent document processing pipelines extract structured entities (tables, images, and text) from documents for use in downstream systems such as knowledge bases, retrieval-augmented generation, and analytics. A persistent limitation of existing pipelines is that extraction output is produced without any intrinsic mechanism to verify whether it faithfully represents the source. Model-internal confidence scores measure inference certainty, not correspondence to the document, and extraction errors pass silently into downstream consumers.
  We present Reconstruction as Validation (RaV-IDP), a document processing pipeline that introduces reconstruction as a first-class architectural component. After each entity is extracted, a dedicated reconstructor renders the extracted representation back into a form comparable to the original document region, and a comparator scores fidelity between the reconstruction and the unmodified source crop. This fidelity score is a grounded, label-free quality signal. When fidelity falls below a per-entity-type threshold, a structured GPT-4.1 vision fallback is triggered and the validation loop repeats. We enforce a bootstrap constraint: the comparator always anchors against the original document region, never against the extraction, preventing the validation from becoming circular.
  We further propose a per-stage evaluation framework pairing each pipeline component with an appropriate benchmark. The code pipeline is publicly available at https://github.com/pritesh-2711/RaV-IDP for experimentation and use.

摘要：智能文檔處理管道從文檔中提取結構化實體（表格、圖像和文本），以供下游系統使用，例如知識庫、檢索增強生成和分析。現有管道的一個持久性限制是，提取輸出是在沒有任何內在機制來驗證其是否忠實於來源的情況下產生的。模型內部的置信度分數衡量推理的確定性，而不是與文檔的對應性，提取錯誤默默地進入下游消費者。

我們提出了重建作為驗證（RaV-IDP），這是一個文檔處理管道，將重建引入為一個一級架構組件。在每個實體被提取後，專門的重建器將提取的表示轉換回與原始文檔區域可比的形式，並且比較器對重建與未修改的來源裁剪之間的忠實度進行評分。這個忠實度分數是一個有根據的、無標籤的質量信號。當忠實度低於每種實體類型的閾值時，會觸發結構化的 GPT-4.1 視覺回退，並重複驗證循環。我們強制執行一個引導約束：比較器始終以原始文檔區域為基準，而不是以提取為基準，防止驗證變得循環。

我們進一步提出了一個每階段評估框架，將每個管道組件與適當的基準配對。代碼管道可在 https://github.com/pritesh-2711/RaV-IDP 上公開獲得，以供實驗和使用。

##### **GraphPlanner: Graph Memory-Augmented Agentic Routing for Multi-Agent LLMs**
2604.23626v1 by Tao Feng, Haozhen Zhang, Zijie Lei, Peixuan Han, Jiaxuan You

LLM routing has achieved promising results in integrating the strengths of diverse models while balancing efficiency and performance. However, to support more realistic and challenging applications, routing must extend into agentic LLM settings, where task planning, multi-round cooperation among heterogeneous agents, and memory utilization are indispensable. To address this gap, we propose GraphPlanner, a heterogeneous graph memory-augmented agentic router for multi-agent LLMs that generates routing workflows for each query and supports both inductive and transductive inference. GraphPlanner formulates workflow generation as a Markov Decision Process (MDP), where at each step it selects both the LLM backbone and the agent role, including Planner, Executor, and Summarizer. By leveraging a heterogeneous graph, denoted as GARNet, to capture interaction memories among queries, agents, and responses, GraphPlanner integrates historical memory and workflow memory into richer state representations. The entire pipeline is optimized with reinforcement learning, jointly improving task-specific performance and computational efficiency. We evaluate GraphPlanner across 14 diverse LLM tasks and demonstrate that: (1) GraphPlanner outperforms strong single-round and multi-round routers, improving accuracy by up to 9.3% while reducing GPU cost from 186.26 GiB to 1.04 GiB; (2) GraphPlanner generalizes robustly to unseen tasks and LLMs, exhibiting strong zero-shot capabilities; and (3) GraphPlanner effectively leverages historical memories, supporting both inductive and transductive inference for more adaptive routing. Our code for GraphPlanner is released at https://github.com/ulab-uiuc/GraphPlanner.

摘要：LLM 路由在整合不同模型的優勢，同時平衡效率和性能方面取得了可喜的成果。<lb/>然而，為了支持更現實和具有挑戰性的應用，路由必須擴展到代理 LLM 設置，其中任務規劃、異質代理之間的多輪合作和記憶利用是不可或缺的。<lb/>為了解決這一空白，我們提出了 GraphPlanner，一種增強異質圖記憶的代理路由器，專為多代理 LLM 設計，能為每個查詢生成路由工作流程，並支持歸納和傳導推理。<lb/>GraphPlanner 將工作流程生成公式化為馬可夫決策過程 (MDP)，在每一步中選擇 LLM 主幹和代理角色，包括規劃者、執行者和摘要者。<lb/>通過利用異質圖，稱為 GARNet，以捕捉查詢、代理和回應之間的互動記憶，GraphPlanner 將歷史記憶和工作流程記憶整合為更豐富的狀態表示。<lb/>整個流程通過強化學習進行優化，聯合改善任務特定性能和計算效率。<lb/>我們在 14 個不同的 LLM 任務中評估了 GraphPlanner，並證明： (1) GraphPlanner 超越了強大的單輪和多輪路由器，準確率提高了最多 9.3%，同時將 GPU 成本從 186.26 GiB 降低到 1.04 GiB； (2) GraphPlanner 對未見任務和 LLM 具有強大的泛化能力，展現出強大的零樣本能力； (3) GraphPlanner 有效利用歷史記憶，支持歸納和傳導推理，以實現更具適應性的路由。我們的 GraphPlanner 代碼已在 https://github.com/ulab-uiuc/GraphPlanner 發布。

##### **ComplianceNLP: Knowledge-Graph-Augmented RAG for Multi-Framework Regulatory Gap Detection**
2604.23585v1 by Dongxin Guo, Jikun Wu, Siu Ming Yiu

Financial institutions must track over 60,000 regulatory events annually, overwhelming manual compliance teams; the industry has paid over USD 300 billion in fines and settlements since the 2008 financial crisis. We present ComplianceNLP, an end-to-end system that automatically monitors regulatory changes, extracts structured obligations, and identifies compliance gaps against institutional policies. The system integrates three components: (1) a knowledge-graph-augmented RAG pipeline grounding generations in a regulatory knowledge graph of 12,847 provisions across SEC, MiFID II, and Basel III; (2) multi-task obligation extraction combining NER, deontic classification, and cross-reference resolution over a shared LEGAL-BERT encoder; and (3) compliance gap analysis that maps obligations to internal policies with severity-aware scoring. On our benchmark, ComplianceNLP achieves 87.7 F1 on gap detection, outperforming GPT-4o+RAG by +3.5 F1, with 94.2% grounding accuracy ($r=0.83$ vs. human judgments) and 83.4 F1 under realistic end-to-end error propagation. Ablations show that knowledge-graph re-ranking contributes the largest marginal gain (+4.6 F1), confirming that structural regulatory knowledge is critical for cross-reference-heavy tasks. Domain-specific knowledge distillation (70B $\to$ 8B) combined with Medusa speculative decoding yields $2.8\times$ inference speedup; regulatory text's low entropy ($H=2.31$ bits vs. $3.87$ general text) produces 91.3% draft-token acceptance rates. In four months of parallel-run deployment processing 9,847 updates at a financial institution, the system achieved 96.0% estimated recall and 90.7% precision, with a $3.1\times$ sustained analyst efficiency gain. We report deployment lessons on trust calibration, GRC integration, and distributional shift monitoring for regulated-domain NLP.

摘要：金融機構每年必須追蹤超過60,000個監管事件，這使得手動合規團隊不堪重負；自2008年金融危機以來，該行業已支付超過3,000億美元的罰款和和解金。<lb/>我們提出了ComplianceNLP，一個端到端的系統，能自動監控監管變更、提取結構化義務，並識別與機構政策之間的合規差距。<lb/>該系統整合了三個組件：(1) 一個知識圖譜增強的RAG管道，將生成內容基於涵蓋12,847條規定的監管知識圖譜，這些規定來自SEC、MiFID II和巴塞爾協議III；(2) 多任務義務提取，結合了NER、義務分類和跨參考解析，使用共享的LEGAL-BERT編碼器；以及(3) 合規差距分析，將義務映射到內部政策並進行嚴重性感知的評分。<lb/>在我們的基準測試中，ComplianceNLP在差距檢測上達到了87.7的F1，超越了GPT-4o+RAG 3.5的F1，並且具有94.2%的基礎準確率（$r=0.83$對比人類判斷）以及在現實端到端錯誤傳播下的83.4 F1。<lb/>消融實驗顯示，知識圖譜重新排序貢獻了最大的邊際增益（+4.6 F1），確認結構性監管知識對於重度跨參考任務至關重要。<lb/>特定領域的知識蒸餾（70B $\to$ 8B）結合Medusa投機解碼實現了$2.8\times$的推理加速；監管文本的低熵（$H=2.31$位對比一般文本的$3.87$）產生了91.3%的草稿標記接受率。<lb/>在四個月的平行運行部署中，處理了9,847次更新，該系統實現了96.0%的預估召回率和90.7%的精確度，並持續提高了$3.1\times$的分析師效率。<lb/>我們報告了在受監管領域的NLP中關於信任校準、GRC整合和分佈變化監控的部署經驗教訓。

##### **AgentEval: DAG-Structured Step-Level Evaluation for Agentic Workflows with Error Propagation Tracking**
2604.23581v1 by Dongxin Guo, Jikun Wu, Siu Ming Yiu

Agentic systems that chain reasoning, tool use, and synthesis into multi-step workflows are entering production, yet prevailing evaluation practices like end-to-end outcome checks and ad-hoc trace inspection systematically mask the intermediate failures that dominate real-world error budgets. We present AgentEval, a framework that formalizes agent executions as evaluation directed acyclic graphs (DAGs), where each node carries typed quality metrics assessed by a calibrated LLM judge (GPT-4o), classified through a hierarchical failure taxonomy (3 levels, 21 subcategories), and linked to upstream dependencies for automated root cause attribution. An ablation study isolates the impact of DAG-based dependency modeling: it alone contributes +22 percentage points to failure detection recall and +34 pp to root cause accuracy over flat step-level evaluation with identical judges and rubrics.
  Across three production workflows (450 test cases, two agent model families, predominantly sequential architectures with a 12% non-DAG trace rate), AgentEval achieves 2.17x higher failure detection recall than end-to-end evaluation (0.89 vs. 0.41), Cohen's kappa = 0.84 agreement with human experts, and 72% root cause accuracy against an 81% human ceiling. Cross-system evaluation on tau-bench and SWE-bench traces confirms transferability (failure detection recall >= 0.78) without taxonomy or rubric modification. A 4-month pilot with 18 engineers detected 23 pre-release regressions through CI/CD-integrated regression testing, reducing median root-cause identification time from 4.2 hours to 22 minutes and driving measurable failure rate reductions in two workflows.

摘要：代理系統將推理、工具使用和綜合整合為多步驟工作流程，正進入生產階段，然而，現行的評估實踐，如端到端結果檢查和臨時追蹤檢查，系統性地掩蓋了主導現實世界錯誤預算的中間失敗。我們提出了AgentEval，一個將代理執行形式化為以評估為導向的有向無環圖（DAG）的框架，其中每個節點攜帶由經過校準的LLM評判（GPT-4o）評估的類型化質量指標，通過分層失敗分類法（3個層級，21個子類別）進行分類，並鏈接到上游依賴項以自動歸因根本原因。一項消融研究隔離了基於DAG的依賴建模的影響：它單獨對失敗檢測召回率貢獻了+22個百分點，對根本原因準確性貢獻了+34個百分點，超過了具有相同評判者和評分標準的平面步驟級評估。在三個生產工作流程中（450個測試案例，兩個代理模型系列，主要是順序架構，具有12%的非DAG追蹤率），AgentEval的失敗檢測召回率比端到端評估高出2.17倍（0.89對0.41），與人類專家的Cohen's kappa = 0.84一致，根本原因準確性為72%，而人類的上限為81%。在tau-bench和SWE-bench追蹤上的跨系統評估確認了可轉移性（失敗檢測召回率 >= 0.78），無需修改分類法或評分標準。為期4個月的試點計劃中，18名工程師通過CI/CD集成的回歸測試檢測到23個發佈前的回歸，將中位根本原因識別時間從4.2小時縮短至22分鐘，並在兩個工作流程中推動可衡量的失敗率降低。

##### **RouteNLP: Closed-Loop LLM Routing with Conformal Cascading and Distillation Co-Optimization**
2604.23577v1 by Dongxin Guo, Jikun Wu, Siu Ming Yiu

Serving diverse NLP workloads with large language models is costly: at one enterprise partner, inference costs exceeded $200K/month despite over 70% of queries being routine tasks well within the capability of smaller models. We present RouteNLP, a closed-loop framework that routes queries across a tiered model portfolio to minimize cost while satisfying per-task quality constraints. The framework integrates three components: a difficulty-aware router with shared task-conditioned representations trained on preference data and quality signals; confidence-calibrated cascading that uses conformal prediction for distribution-free threshold initialization; and a distillation-routing co-optimization loop that clusters escalation failures, applies targeted knowledge distillation to cheaper models, and automatically retrains the router, yielding over twice the cost improvement of untargeted distillation. In an 8-week pilot deployment processing ~5K queries/day at an enterprise customer-service division, RouteNLP reduced inference costs by 58% while maintaining 91% response acceptance and reducing p99 latency from 1,847 ms to 387 ms. On a six-task benchmark spanning finance, customer service, and legal domains, the framework achieves 40-85% cost reduction while retaining 96-100% quality on structured tasks and 96-98% on generation tasks, with human evaluation confirming that 74.5% of routed generation outputs match or exceed frontier-model quality.

摘要：提供多樣化的自然語言處理工作負載與大型語言模型的成本高昂：在一個企業合作夥伴中，推理成本超過每月 20 萬美元，儘管超過 70% 的查詢是常規任務，這些任務完全在較小模型的能力範圍內。我們提出了 RouteNLP，一個閉環框架，通過分層模型組合路由查詢，以最小化成本，同時滿足每個任務的質量約束。該框架整合了三個組件：一個基於難度的路由器，具有基於偏好數據和質量信號訓練的共享任務條件表示；使用符合預測進行無分佈閾值初始化的信心校準級聯；以及一個蒸餾路由共同優化循環，聚類升級失敗，對較便宜的模型應用有針對性的知識蒸餾，並自動重新訓練路由器，實現了超過未針對性蒸餾的兩倍成本改善。在一個為期 8 週的試點部署中，處理約 5,000 條查詢/天於一家企業客戶服務部門，RouteNLP 將推理成本降低了 58%，同時保持 91% 的回應接受率，並將 p99 延遲從 1,847 毫秒降低到 387 毫秒。在一個涵蓋金融、客戶服務和法律領域的六任務基準中，該框架實現了 40-85% 的成本降低，同時在結構化任務上保持 96-100% 的質量，在生成任務上保持 96-98% 的質量，並且人類評估確認 74.5% 的路由生成輸出達到或超過前沿模型的質量。

##### **COMO: Closed-Loop Optical Molecule Recognition with Minimum Risk Training**
2604.23546v1 by Zhuoqi Lyu, Qing Ke

Optical chemical structure recognition (OCSR) translates molecular images into machine-readable representations like SMILES strings or molecular graphs, but remains challenging in real-world documents due to inexhaustible variations in chemical structures, shorthand conventions, and visual noise. Most existing deep-learning-based approaches rely on teacher forcing with token-level Maximum Likelihood Estimation (MLE). This training paradigm suffers from exposure bias, as models are trained under ground-truth prefixes but must condition on their own previous predictions during inference. Moreover, token-level MLE objectives hinder the optimization towards molecular-level evaluation criteria such as chemical validity and structural similarity. Here we introduce Minimum Risk Training (MRT) to OCSR and propose COMO (Closed-loop Optical Molecule recOgnition), a closed-loop framework that mitigates exposure bias by directly optimizing over molecule-level, non-differentiable objectives, by iteratively sampling and evaluating the model's own predictions. Experiments on ten benchmarks including synthetic and real-world chemical diagrams from patent and scientific literature demonstrate that COMO substantially outperforms existing rule-based and learning-based methods with less training data. Ablation studies further show that MRT is architecture-agnostic, demonstrating its potential for broad application to end-to-end OCSR systems.

摘要：光學化學結構識別 (OCSR) 將分子圖像轉換為機器可讀的表示形式，例如 SMILES 字串或分子圖，但在現實世界的文件中仍然面臨挑戰，因為化學結構、簡寫慣例和視覺噪聲的變化無窮無盡。大多數現有的基於深度學習的方法依賴於使用標記級最大似然估計 (MLE) 的教師強迫。這種訓練範式受到曝光偏見的困擾，因為模型是在真實前綴下進行訓練的，但在推斷過程中必須依賴自己之前的預測。此外，標記級 MLE 目標妨礙了對分子級評估標準（如化學有效性和結構相似性）的優化。在此，我們將最小風險訓練 (MRT) 引入 OCSR，並提出 COMO（閉環光學分子識別），這是一個閉環框架，通過直接優化分子級的非可微目標來減輕曝光偏見，並通過迭代抽樣和評估模型自己的預測。對十個基準的實驗，包括來自專利和科學文獻的合成和現實世界的化學圖表，證明 COMO 在訓練數據較少的情況下顯著優於現有的基於規則和基於學習的方法。消融研究進一步顯示 MRT 是架構無關的，顯示其在端到端 OCSR 系統中的廣泛應用潛力。

##### **Do Transaction-Level and Actor-Level AML Queues Agree? An Empirical Evaluation of Granularity Effects on the Elliptic++ Graph**
2604.23494v1 by Ankur Malik

Graph-based anti-money laundering (AML) systems on blockchain networks can score suspicious activity at two granularity levels -- transactions or actor addresses -- yet compliance action is conducted per actor. This paper contributes an evaluation methodology for measuring how scoring granularity affects investigation queue composition under fixed review budgets. We formalize the evaluation through a projection framework mapping transaction-level scores to the actor-level action unit via four aggregation operators, and introduce budgeted investigation metrics -- yield@budget, burden decomposition, and case fragmentation. Using the public Elliptic++ Bitcoin dataset (203,769 transactions; 822,942 address occurrences), we train independent random forest classifiers at each level under a causal temporal protocol and compare review queues through Jaccard overlap, burden decomposition, and feature-matching ablations. At one-percent budget, temporal evaluation yields mean Jaccard of 0.374 (SD 0.171); static pooled evaluation yields 0.087 (95% CI [0.079, 0.094]). An enriched address model receiving all 237 features produces even lower overlap (Jaccard=0.051), with 4.3% illicit per 100 reviews versus 30.2% for the transaction-projected queue. Address-level detection value is temporally concentrated: two timesteps exceed 91% illicit per 100 reviews while the static burden is only 3.4%. A fixed hybrid policy underperforms the best single-level queue by 5.05pp (CI [-10.2pp, -0.9pp]). These findings establish that scoring granularity is a consequential design variable for AML investigation systems -- same data, same budget, different queues, different addresses investigated.

摘要：基於圖形的反洗錢 (AML) 系統在區塊鏈網絡上可以在兩個粒度層級上評分可疑活動——交易或行為者地址——但合規行動是根據行為者進行的。本文貢獻了一種評估方法，用於測量評分粒度如何影響在固定審查預算下的調查隊列組成。我們通過一個投影框架形式化評估，將交易層級的分數映射到行為者層級的行動單位，並通過四個聚合運算子引入預算調查指標——yield@budget、負擔分解和案件碎片化。使用公共的 Elliptic++ 比特幣數據集（203,769 笔交易；822,942 地址出現），我們在因果時間協議下對每個層級訓練獨立的隨機森林分類器，並通過 Jaccard 重疊、負擔分解和特徵匹配消融比較審查隊列。在一百分之一的預算下，時間評估的平均 Jaccard 為 0.374（標準差 0.171）；靜態池評估為 0.087（95% 置信區間 [0.079, 0.094]）。接收所有 237 個特徵的增強地址模型產生了更低的重疊（Jaccard=0.051），每 100 次審查中有 4.3% 的非法活動，與交易投影隊列的 30.2% 相比。地址層級的檢測價值在時間上是集中性的：兩個時間步驟每 100 次審查中超過 91% 的非法活動，而靜態負擔僅為 3.4%。固定混合政策的表現比最佳單層隊列低 5.05 個百分點（置信區間 [-10.2pp, -0.9pp]）。這些發現確立了評分粒度是反洗錢調查系統的一個重要設計變量——相同數據、相同預算、不同隊列、不同地址被調查。

##### **K-SENSE: A Knowledge-Guided Self-Augmented Encoder for Neuro-Semantic Evaluation of Mental Health Conditions on Social Media**
2604.23493v2 by Vijay Yadav

Early detection of mental health conditions, particularly stress and depression, from social media text remains a challenging open problem in computational psychiatry and natural language processing. Automated systems must contend with figurative language, implicit emotional expression, and the high noise inherent in user-generated content. Existing approaches either leverage external commonsense knowledge to model mental states explicitly, or apply self-augmentation and contrastive training to improve generalization, but seldom do both in a principled, unified framework. We propose K-SENSE (Knowledge-guided Self-augmented Encoder for Neuro-Semantic Evaluation of Mental Health), a framework that jointly exploits external psychological reasoning and internal representation robustness. K-SENSE adopts a three-stage encoding pipeline: (1) inferential commonsense knowledge is extracted from the COMET model across five mental state dimensions; (2) a semantic anchor is constructed by combining hidden representations from two parallel encoding streams, projected into a shared space before fusion; and (3) a supervised contrastive learning objective aligns same-class representations while encouraging the attention mechanism to suppress irrelevant knowledge noise. We evaluate K-SENSE on Dreaddit (stress detection) and Depression_Mixed (depression detection), achieving mean F1-scores of 86.1 (0.6%) and 94.3 (0.8%), respectively, over five independent runs. These represent improvements of approximately 2.6 and 1.5 percentage points over the strongest prior baselines. Ablation experiments confirm the contribution of each architectural component, including the temporal knowledge integration strategy and the choice to keep the knowledge encoder frozen during fine-tuning.

摘要：早期從社交媒體文本中檢測心理健康狀況，特別是壓力和抑鬱，仍然是計算精神病學和自然語言處理中的一個挑戰性開放問題。<lb/>自動化系統必須應對比喻語言、隱含情感表達以及用戶生成內容中固有的高噪聲。<lb/>現有的方法要麼利用外部常識知識來明確建模心理狀態，要麼應用自我增強和對比訓練來提高泛化能力，但很少在一個有原則的統一框架中同時做到這兩點。<lb/>我們提出了 K-SENSE（知識引導的自我增強編碼器，用於心理健康的神經語義評估），這是一個共同利用外部心理推理和內部表示穩健性的框架。<lb/>K-SENSE 採用三階段編碼管道：<lb/>(1) 從 COMET 模型中提取推理常識知識，涵蓋五個心理狀態維度；<lb/>(2) 通過將來自兩個平行編碼流的隱藏表示結合來構建語義錨點，然後投影到共享空間再進行融合；<lb/>(3) 監督對比學習目標對齊同類表示，同時鼓勵注意機制抑制無關的知識噪聲。<lb/>我們在 Dreaddit（壓力檢測）和 Depression_Mixed（抑鬱檢測）上評估 K-SENSE，分別達到 86.1（0.6%）和 94.3（0.8%）的平均 F1 分數，這是五次獨立運行的結果。<lb/>這些分數分別比最強的先前基準提高了約 2.6 和 1.5 個百分點。<lb/>消融實驗確認了每個架構組件的貢獻，包括時間知識整合策略和在微調過程中保持知識編碼器凍結的選擇。

##### **Hybrid JIT-CUDA Graph Optimization for Low-Latency Large Language Model Inference**
2604.23467v1 by Divakar Kumar Yadav, Tian Zhao

Large Language Models (LLMs) have achieved strong performance across natural language and multimodal tasks, yet their practical deployment remains constrained by inference latency and kernel launch overhead, particularly in interactive, short-sequence settings. This paper presents a hybrid runtime framework that combines Just-In-Time (JIT) compilation with CUDA Graph execution to reduce launch overhead while preserving runtime flexibility during autoregressive decoding. The framework partitions transformer inference into static components executed via CUDA Graph replay and dynamic components handled through JIT-compiled kernels, enabling asynchronous graph capture and reuse across decoding steps.
  We evaluate the proposed approach on LLaMA-2 7B using single-GPU, batch-size-one inference across prompt lengths from 10 to 500 tokens. Experimental results show that the hybrid runtime reduces Time-to-First-Token (TTFT) by up to 66.0% and achieves lower P99 latency compared with TensorRT-LLM in this regime. These results indicate that hybrid JIT-CUDA Graph execution can effectively reduce inference latency and variance for short-sequence LLM workloads, making it a practical optimization strategy for latency-sensitive AI applications.

摘要：大型語言模型（LLMs）在自然語言和多模態任務中表現出色，但其實際部署仍受限於推理延遲和內核啟動開銷，特別是在互動式的短序列環境中。本文提出了一種混合運行時框架，將即時編譯（Just-In-Time, JIT）與CUDA圖執行相結合，以減少啟動開銷，同時在自回歸解碼過程中保持運行時靈活性。該框架將Transformer推理劃分為通過CUDA圖重播執行的靜態組件和通過JIT編譯內核處理的動態組件，從而實現解碼步驟之間的異步圖捕獲和重用。<lb/>我們在LLaMA-2 7B上評估了所提出的方法，使用單GPU、批次大小為1的推理，涵蓋從10到500個標記的提示長度。實驗結果顯示，混合運行時將首次標記時間（Time-to-First-Token, TTFT）減少了最多66.0%，並在此範疇內實現了較低的P99延遲。這些結果表明，混合JIT-CUDA圖執行可以有效減少短序列LLM工作負載的推理延遲和變異性，成為對延遲敏感的AI應用的一種實用優化策略。

##### **IndustryAssetEQA: A Neurosymbolic Operational Intelligence System for Embodied Question Answering in Industrial Asset Maintenance**
2604.23446v1 by Chathurangi Shyalika, Dhaval Patel, Amit Sheth

Industrial maintenance environments increasingly rely on AI systems to assist operators in understanding asset behavior, diagnosing failures, and evaluating interventions. Although large language models (LLMs) enable fluent natural-language interaction, deployed maintenance assistants routinely produce generic explanations that are weakly grounded in telemetry, omit verifiable provenance, and offer no testable support for counterfactual or action-oriented reasoning that undermine trust in safety-critical settings. We present IndustryAssetEQA, a neurosymbolic operational intelligence system that combines episodic telemetry representations with a Failure Mode Effects Analysis Knowledge Graph (FMEA-KG) to enable Embodied Question Answering (EQA) over industrial assets. 摘要：工業維護環境越來越依賴人工智慧系統來協助操作員理解資產行為、診斷故障和評估干預措施。儘管大型語言模型（LLMs）能夠實現流暢的自然語言互動，但已部署的維護助手常常產生基於遙測的薄弱解釋，省略可驗證的來源，並且對反事實或以行動為導向的推理不提供可測試的支持，這在安全關鍵的環境中削弱了信任。我們提出了IndustryAssetEQA，一個神經符號運營智能系統，將情節遙測表示與故障模式影響分析知識圖譜（FMEA-KG）結合，以實現對工業資產的具身問答（EQA）。我們在四個數據集上進行評估，涵蓋四種工業資產類型，包括旋轉機械、渦扇發動機、液壓系統和網絡物理生產系統。與僅使用LLM的基準相比，IndustryAssetEQA在結構有效性上提高了最多0.51，在反事實準確性上提高了最多0.47，在解釋推理上提高了0.64，同時將專家評定的過度聲稱從28%降低到2%（約93%的減少）。代碼、數據集和FMEA-KG可在https://github.com/IBM/AssetOpsBench/tree/IndustryAssetEQA/IndustryAssetEQA獲得。

##### **Automating Categorization of Scientific Texts with In-Context Learning and Prompt-Chaining in Large Language Models**
2604.23430v1 by Gautam Kishore Shahi, Oliver Hummel

The relentless expansion of scientific literature presents significant challenges for navigation and knowledge discovery. Within Research Information Retrieval, established tasks such as text summarization and classification remain crucial for enabling researchers and practitioners to effectively navigate this vast landscape, so that efforts have increasingly been focused on developing advanced research information systems. These systems aim not only to provide standard keyword-based search functionalities but also to incorporate capabilities for automatic content categorization within knowledge-intensive organizations across academia and industry. This study systematically evaluates the performance of off-the-shelf Large Language Models (LLMs) in analyzing scientific texts according to a given classification scheme. We utilized the hierarchical ORKG taxonomy as a classification framework, employing the FORC dataset as ground truth. We investigated the effectiveness of advanced prompt engineering strategies, namely In-Context Learning (ICL) and Prompt Chaining, and experimentally explored the influence of the LLMs' temperature hyperparameter on classification accuracy. Our experiments demonstrate that Prompt Chaining yields superior classification accuracy compared to pure ICL, particularly when applied to the nested structure of the ORKG taxonomy. LLMs with prompt chaining outperform the state-of-the-art models for domain (1st level) prediction and show even better performance for subject (2nd level) prediction compared to the older BERT model. However, LLMs are not yet able to perform well in classifying the topic (3rd level) of research areas based on this specific hierarchical taxonomy, as they only reach about 50% accuracy even with prompt chaining.
