##### **Evolve: A Persistent Knowledge Lifecycle for Small Language Models**
2604.23424v1 by Dikran Hovagimian

Evolve pairs a small local language model with a persistent, teacher-compiled knowledge store -- refined through sleep consolidation and usage-driven refresh -- to deliver substantial accuracy gains over the model's parametric baseline while amortizing teacher costs through cross-query knowledge reuse. Rather than retrieving document fragments at query time, Evolve constructs a store of semantically coherent sections compiled by teacher models at natural conceptual boundaries; new sections are staged on acquisition, consolidated offline through teacher-mediated merging, and refreshed inline when expired. A 2B-parameter local model handles classification and generation; large teacher models are invoked only for knowledge operations.
  Across 750 benchmark queries spanning custom specialist questions, NaturalQuestions, and TriviaQA, the 2B model augmented by Evolve improves from 20-33% baseline accuracy to 60-84% (+40-52pp) while reducing teacher invocations by over 50% through reuse. Post-consolidation compresses the knowledge store by 31-33.5% across three independent benchmarks while preserving accuracy; section-based retrieval outperforms chunk-based retrieval by 5-9pp across every lifecycle condition. The architecture supports two generation modes over the same lifecycle -- suppress (strict section-only grounding, auditable) and augment (section-supplemented responses).

摘要：Evolve 將一個小型本地語言模型與一個持久的、由教師編輯的知識庫相結合——通過睡眠鞏固和使用驅動的刷新進行精煉——以在模型的參數基準上實現顯著的準確性提升，同時通過跨查詢知識重用來攤銷教師成本。Evolve 並不是在查詢時檢索文檔片段，而是構建一個由教師模型在自然概念邊界編輯的語義一致部分的庫；新部分在獲取時進行階段性處理，通過教師介導的合併進行線下鞏固，並在過期時進行內聯刷新。一個 2B 參數的本地模型處理分類和生成；大型教師模型僅在知識操作時被調用。<lb/>在涵蓋自定義專家問題、NaturalQuestions 和 TriviaQA 的 750 個基準查詢中，Evolve 增強的 2B 模型將基準準確率從 20-33% 提升到 60-84%（+40-52pp），同時通過重用將教師調用減少超過 50%。後鞏固使知識庫在三個獨立基準上壓縮了 31-33.5%，同時保持準確性；基於部分的檢索在每個生命周期條件下均超過基於片段的檢索 5-9pp。該架構支持在相同生命周期內的兩種生成模式——抑制（嚴格的僅部分基礎，便於審計）和增強（部分補充的回應）。

##### **Beyond Local vs. External: A Game-Theoretic Framework for Trustworthy Knowledge Acquisition**
2604.23413v1 by Rujing Yao, Yufei Shi, Yang Wu, Ang Li, Zhuoren Jiang, XiaoFeng Wang, Haixu Tang, Xiaozhong Liu

Cloud-hosted Large Language Models (LLMs) offer unmatched reasoning capabilities and dynamic knowledge, yet submitting raw queries to these external services risks exposing sensitive user intent. Conversely, relying exclusively on trusted local models preserves privacy but often compromises answer quality due to limited parameter scale and knowledge. To resolve this dilemma, we propose Game-theoretic Trustworthy Knowledge Acquisition (GTKA), a framework that formulates the trade-off between knowledge utility and privacy as a strategic game. GTKA consists of three components: (i) a privacy-aware sub-query generator that decomposes sensitive intent into generalized, low-risk fragments; (ii) an adversarial reconstruction attacker that attempts to infer the original query from these fragments, providing adaptive leakage signals; and (iii) a trusted local integrator that synthesizes external responses within a secure boundary. By training the generator and attacker in an alternating adversarial manner, GTKA optimizes the sub-query generation policy to maximize knowledge acquisition accuracy while minimizing the reconstructability of the original sensitive intent. To validate our approach, we construct two sensitive-domain benchmarks in the biomedical and legal fields. Extensive experiments demonstrate that GTKA significantly reduces intent leakage compared to state-of-the-art baselines while maintaining high-fidelity answer quality.

摘要：雲端托管的大型語言模型（LLMs）提供無與倫比的推理能力和動態知識，但向這些外部服務提交原始查詢會冒著暴露敏感用戶意圖的風險。相反，完全依賴受信的本地模型雖然能夠保護隱私，但由於參數規模和知識的限制，往往會妥協答案質量。為了解決這一困境，我們提出了博弈論的可信知識獲取（GTKA）框架，將知識效用與隱私之間的權衡表述為一個策略性遊戲。GTKA 由三個組件組成：（i）一個隱私意識的子查詢生成器，將敏感意圖分解為一般化的低風險片段；（ii）一個對抗性重建攻擊者，試圖從這些片段推斷原始查詢，提供自適應的洩漏信號；以及（iii）一個可信的本地整合器，在安全邊界內合成外部響應。通過以交替對抗的方式訓練生成器和攻擊者，GTKA 優化了子查詢生成策略，以最大化知識獲取的準確性，同時最小化原始敏感意圖的可重建性。為了驗證我們的方法，我們在生物醫學和法律領域構建了兩個敏感領域基準。廣泛的實驗表明，與最先進的基準相比，GTKA 顯著降低了意圖洩漏，同時保持了高保真度的答案質量。

##### **SoccerRef-Agents: Multi-Agent System for Automated Soccer Refereeing**
2604.23392v1 by Zi Meng, Wanli Song, Yi Hu, Jiayuan Rao, Gang Chen

Refereeing is vital in sports, where fair, accurate, and explainable decisions are fundamental. While intelligent assistant technologies are being widely adopted in soccer refereeing, current AI-assisted approaches remain preliminary. Existing research mostly focuses on isolated video perception tasks and lacks the ability to understand and reason about foul scenarios. To fill this gap, we propose SoccerRef-Agents, a holistic and explainable multi-agent decision-making framework for soccer refereeing. The main contributions are: (i) constructing the multimodal benchmark SoccerRefBench with over 1,200 referee theory questions and 600 foul video clips; (ii) building a vector-based knowledge base RefKnowledgeDB using the latest "Laws of the Game" and a classic case database for precise, knowledge-driven reasoning; (iii) designing a novel multi-agent architecture that collaborates via cross-modal RAG to bridge the semantic gap between visual content and regulatory texts. This work explores the technical capability of integrating MLLMs with refereeing expertise, and evaluations show our system significantly outperforms general-purpose MLLMs in decision accuracy and explanation quality. All databases, benchmarks, and code will be made available.

摘要：裁判在體育運動中至關重要，公正、準確且可解釋的決策是基本要求。雖然智能助手技術在足球裁判中被廣泛採用，但目前的 AI 輔助方法仍然處於初步階段。現有研究主要集中在孤立的視頻感知任務上，缺乏理解和推理犯規情境的能力。為了填補這一空白，我們提出了 SoccerRef-Agents，這是一個全面且可解釋的多代理決策框架，用於足球裁判。主要貢獻包括：(i) 構建多模態基準 SoccerRefBench，包含超過 1,200 道裁判理論問題和 600 段犯規視頻剪輯；(ii) 建立基於向量的知識庫 RefKnowledgeDB，使用最新的《比賽規則》和一個經典案例數據庫，以實現精確的知識驅動推理；(iii) 設計一種新穎的多代理架構，通過跨模態 RAG 協作，彌合視覺內容與規範文本之間的語義差距。這項工作探索了將 MLLMs 與裁判專業知識整合的技術能力，評估顯示我們的系統在決策準確性和解釋質量上顯著超越通用 MLLMs。所有數據庫、基準和代碼將會公開。

##### **A Parametric Memory Head for Continual Generative Retrieval**
2604.23388v1 by Kidist Amde Mekonnen, Yubao Tang, Maarten de Rijke

Generative information retrieval (GenIR) consolidates retrieval into a single neural model that decodes document identifiers (docids) directly from queries. While this model-as-index paradigm offers architectural simplicity, it is poorly suited to dynamic document collections. Unlike modular systems, where indexes are easily updated, GenIR's knowledge is parametrically encoded in its weights; consequently, standard adaptation methods such as full and parameter-efficient fine-tuning can induce catastrophic forgetting. We show that sequential adaptation improves retrieval on newly added documents but substantially degrades performance on earlier slices, exposing a pronounced stability-plasticity trade-off. To address this, we propose post-adaptation memory tuning (PAMT), a memory-only stabilization stage that augments an adapted model with a modular parametric memory head (PMH). PAMT freezes the backbone and attaches a product-key memory with fixed addressing. During prefix-trie constrained decoding, decoder hidden states sparsely query PMH to produce residual corrections in hidden space; these corrections are mapped to score adjustments via the frozen output embedding matrix, computed only over trie-valid tokens. This guides docid generation while keeping routing and backbone parameters fixed. To limit cross-slice interference, PAMT updates only a fixed budget of memory values selected using decoding-time access statistics, prioritizing entries frequently activated by the current slice and rarely used in prior sessions. Experiments on MS MARCO and Natural Questions under sequential, disjoint corpus increments show that PAMT substantially improves retention on earlier slices with minimal impact on retrieval performance for newly added documents, while modifying only a sparse subset of memory values per session.

摘要：生成資訊檢索（GenIR）將檢索整合為一個單一的神經模型，該模型直接從查詢中解碼文檔識別碼（docids）。雖然這種模型作為索引的範式提供了架構上的簡單性，但它並不適合動態文檔集合。與模組化系統不同，模組化系統的索引可以輕鬆更新，GenIR 的知識是以參數形式編碼在其權重中；因此，標準的適應方法，如完全和參數高效的微調，可能會導致災難性遺忘。我們顯示，序列適應在新添加的文檔上改善了檢索，但對早期片段的性能造成了顯著下降，暴露出明顯的穩定性-可塑性權衡。為了解決這個問題，我們提出了後適應記憶調整（PAMT），這是一個僅限記憶的穩定化階段，通過模組化的參數記憶頭（PMH）來增強適應後的模型。PAMT 冷凍了主幹並附加了一個具有固定尋址的產品鍵記憶。在前綴樹約束解碼過程中，解碼器隱藏狀態稀疏地查詢 PMH，以在隱藏空間中產生殘差修正；這些修正通過冷凍的輸出嵌入矩陣映射到分數調整，僅在樹有效的標記上計算。這指導了 docid 的生成，同時保持路由和主幹參數固定。為了限制跨片段的干擾，PAMT 僅更新使用解碼時訪問統計選擇的固定預算的記憶值，優先考慮當前片段經常激活的條目以及在先前會話中很少使用的條目。在 MS MARCO 和自然問題的實驗中，通過序列的、不重疊的語料庫增量顯示，PAMT 顯著改善了早期片段的保留，對新添加文檔的檢索性能影響最小，同時每個會話僅修改一個稀疏的記憶值子集。

##### **GSAR: Typed Grounding for Hallucination Detection and Recovery in Multi-Agent LLMs**
2604.23366v1 by Federico A. Kamelhar

Autonomous multi-agent LLM systems are increasingly deployed to investigate operational incidents and produce structured diagnostic reports. Their trustworthiness hinges on whether each claim is grounded in observed evidence rather than model-internal inference. Existing groundedness evaluators (binary classifiers, LLM-as-judge scalars, self-correction loops) treat supporting evidence as interchangeable and emit a single signal that offers no principled control over downstream action.
  We present GSAR, a grounding-evaluation and replanning framework that (i) partitions claims into a four-way typology (grounded, ungrounded, contradicted, complementary), giving first-class standing to non-redundant alternative perspectives; (ii) assigns evidence-type-specific weights reflecting epistemic strength; (iii) computes an asymmetric contradiction-penalised weighted groundedness score; and (iv) couples that score to a three-tier decision function (proceed, regenerate, replan) driving a bounded-iteration outer loop under an explicit compute budget.
  We formalise the algorithm, prove six structural properties, and evaluate five design claims on FEVER with gold Wikipedia evidence under four independently-trained LLM judges (gpt-5.4, claude-sonnet-4-6, claude-opus-4-7, gemini-2.5-pro). Every ablation reproduces in the same direction on every judge: bootstrap 95% CIs on the rho=0 effect exclude 0 on all four; the no-complementary ablation under Opus 4.7 has CI [-96,-68] of 200; at n=1000 three independent judges converge to DeltaS(rho=0)=+0.058. A head-to-head against Vectara HHEM-2.1-Open is included. To our knowledge, GSAR is the first published groundedness framework coupling evidence-typed scoring with tiered recovery under an explicit compute budget.

摘要：自主多代理LLM系統越來越多地被用來調查操作事件並生成結構化的診斷報告。它們的可信度取決於每一個主張是否基於觀察到的證據，而不是模型內部的推斷。現有的基礎評估器（二元分類器、LLM作為評判者的標量、自我修正循環）將支持證據視為可互換，並發出單一信號，這對下游行動沒有原則性的控制。<lb/>  
我們提出了GSAR，一個基礎評估和重新規劃框架，(i) 將主張劃分為四種類型（有根據、無根據、相互矛盾、互補），賦予非冗餘替代觀點一級地位；(ii) 指派特定證據類型的權重，反映認識強度；(iii) 計算一個不對稱的矛盾懲罰加權基礎分數；(iv) 將該分數與一個三級決策函數（繼續、再生、重新規劃）結合，驅動在明確計算預算下的有限迭代外部循環。<lb/>  
我們形式化了該算法，證明了六個結構性質，並在FEVER上使用四個獨立訓練的LLM評判者（gpt-5.4、claude-sonnet-4-6、claude-opus-4-7、gemini-2.5-pro）對五個設計主張進行了評估。每個消融在每個評判者上都朝著相同的方向重現：在rho=0的效應上，bootstrap 95% CIs排除了所有四個評判者的0；在Opus 4.7下的無互補消融有CI [-96,-68]的200；在n=1000時，三個獨立評判者收斂到DeltaS(rho=0)=+0.058。還包括了一個與Vectara HHEM-2.1-Open的正面對決。據我們所知，GSAR是第一個發表的基礎框架，將證據類型的評分與在明確計算預算下的分層恢復結合在一起。

##### **VeriLLMed: Interactive Visual Debugging of Medical Large Language Models with Knowledge Graphs**
2604.23356v1 by Yurui Xiang, Xingyi Mao, Rui Sheng, Zixin Chen, Zelin Zang, Yuyang Wu, Haipeng Zeng, Huamin Qu, Yushi Sun, Yanna Lin

Large language models (LLMs) show promise in medical diagnosis, but real-world deployment remains challenging due to high-stakes clinical decisions and imperfect reasoning reliability. As a result, careful inspection of model behavior is essential for assessing whether diagnostic reasoning is reliable and clinically grounded. However, debugging medical LLMs remains difficult. First, developers often lack sufficient medical domain expertise to interpret model errors in clinically meaningful terms. Second, models can fail across a large and diverse set of instances involving different input types, tasks, and reasoning steps, making it challenging for developers to prioritize which errors deserve focused inspection. Third, developers struggle to identify recurring error patterns across cases, as existing debugging practices are largely instance-centric and rely on manual inspection of isolated failures. To address these challenges, we present VeriLLMed, a visual analytics system that integrates external biomedical knowledge to audit and debug medical LLM diagnostic reasoning. VeriLLMed transforms model outputs into comparable reasoning paths, constructs knowledge graph-grounded reference paths, and identifies three recurring classes of diagnosis errors: relation errors, branch errors, and missing errors. Case studies and expert evaluation demonstrate that VeriLLMed helps developers identify clinically implausible reasoning and generate actionable insights that can inform the improvement of medical LLMs.

摘要：大型語言模型（LLMs）在醫療診斷中顯示出潛力，但由於高風險的臨床決策和不完善的推理可靠性，實際應用仍然具有挑戰性。<lb/>因此，仔細檢查模型行為對於評估診斷推理是否可靠且臨床基礎至關重要。<lb/>然而，調試醫療LLMs仍然困難重重。<lb/>首先，開發者通常缺乏足夠的醫學領域專業知識，無法以臨床意義解釋模型錯誤。<lb/>其次，模型可能在涉及不同輸入類型、任務和推理步驟的大量多樣實例中失敗，這使得開發者難以優先考慮哪些錯誤值得重點檢查。<lb/>第三，開發者難以識別跨案例的重複錯誤模式，因為現有的調試實踐主要以實例為中心，並依賴於對孤立失敗的手動檢查。<lb/>為了解決這些挑戰，我們提出了VeriLLMed，一個視覺分析系統，該系統整合了外部生物醫學知識，以審核和調試醫療LLM的診斷推理。<lb/>VeriLLMed將模型輸出轉換為可比較的推理路徑，構建基於知識圖譜的參考路徑，並識別三類重複的診斷錯誤：關係錯誤、分支錯誤和缺失錯誤。<lb/>案例研究和專家評估表明，VeriLLMed幫助開發者識別臨床上不合理的推理，並生成可行的見解，這些見解可以促進醫療LLMs的改進。

##### **Bridging Reasoning and Action: Hybrid LLM-RL Framework for Efficient Cross-Domain Task-Oriented Dialogue**
2604.23345v1 by Yangyang Zhao, Linfan Dai, Li Cai, Bowen Xing, Libo Qin

Cross-domain task-oriented dialogue requires reasoning over implicit and explicit feasibility constraints while planning long-horizon, multi-turn actions. Large language models (LLMs) can infer such constraints but are unreliable over long horizons, while Reinforcement learning (RL) optimizes long-horizon behavior yet cannot recover constraints from raw dialogue. Naively coupling LLMs with RL is therefore brittle: unverified or unstructured LLM outputs can corrupt state representations and misguide policy learning. Motivated by this, we propose Verified LLM-Knowledge empowered RL (VLK-RL), a hybrid framework that makes LLM-derived constraint reasoning usable for RL. VLK-RL first elicits candidate constraints with an LLM and then verifies them via a dual-role cross-examination procedure to suppress hallucinations and cross-turn inconsistencies. The verified constraints are mapped into ontology-aligned slot-value representations, yielding a structured, constraint-aware state for RL policy optimization. Experiments across multiple benchmarks demonstrate that VLK-RL significantly improves generalization and robustness, outperforming strong single-model baselines on long-horizon tasks.

摘要：跨域任務導向對話需要在規劃長期、多輪行動時，對隱含和明確的可行性約束進行推理。大型語言模型（LLMs）能夠推斷這些約束，但在長期範圍內不可靠，而強化學習（RL）則優化長期行為，但無法從原始對話中恢復約束。因此，將LLMs與RL簡單結合是脆弱的：未經驗證或結構不良的LLM輸出可能會破壞狀態表示並誤導策略學習。受到這一點的啟發，我們提出了經過驗證的LLM知識增強RL（VLK-RL），這是一個混合框架，使LLM衍生的約束推理可用於RL。VLK-RL首先利用LLM引出候選約束，然後通過雙重角色交叉檢查程序驗證它們，以抑制幻覺和跨輪不一致性。經過驗證的約束被映射到本體對齊的槽值表示中，產生一個結構化的、具約束意識的狀態，以便於RL策略優化。在多個基準測試中的實驗表明，VLK-RL顯著提高了泛化能力和穩健性，在長期任務上超越了強大的單模型基準。

##### **EAD-Net: Emotion-Aware Talking Head Generation with Spatial Refinement and Temporal Coherence**
2604.23325v1 by Yahui Li, Yinfeng Yu, Liejun Wang, Shengjie Shen

Emotionally talking head video generation aims to generate expressive portrait videos with accurate lip synchronization and emotional facial expressions. Current methods rely on simple emotional labels, leading to insufficient semantic information. While introducing high-level semantics enhances expressiveness, it easily causes lip-sync degradation. Furthermore, mainstream generation methods struggle to balance computational efficiency and global motion awareness in long videos and suffer from poor temporal coherence. Therefore, we propose an \textbf{E}motion-\textbf{A}ware \textbf{D}iffusion model-based \textbf{Net}work, called \textbf{EAD-Net}. We introduce SyncNet supervision and Temporal Representation Alignment (TREPA) to mitigate lip-sync degradation caused by multi-modal fusion. To model complex spatio-temporal dependencies in long video sequences, we propose a Spatio-Temporal Directional Attention (STDA) mechanism that captures global motion patterns through strip attention. Additionally, we design a Temporal Frame graph Reasoning Module (TFRM) to explicitly model temporal coherence between video frames through graph structure learning. To enhance emotional semantic control, a large language model is employed to extract textual descriptions from real videos, serving as high-level semantic guidance. Experiments on the HDTF and MEAD datasets demonstrate that our method outperforms existing methods in terms of lip-sync accuracy, temporal consistency, and emotional accuracy.

摘要：情感對話頭影片生成旨在生成具有準確嘴唇同步和情感面部表情的表現力肖像影片。當前的方法依賴於簡單的情感標籤，導致語義信息不足。雖然引入高級語義可以增強表現力，但也容易導致嘴唇同步的退化。此外，主流生成方法在長影片中難以平衡計算效率和全局運動感知，並且存在時間一致性差的問題。因此，我們提出了一種基於\textbf{E}motion-\textbf{A}ware \textbf{D}iffusion模型的\textbf{Net}work，稱為\textbf{EAD-Net}。我們引入SyncNet監督和時間表示對齊（TREPA）來減輕由多模態融合引起的嘴唇同步退化。為了建模長影片序列中的複雜時空依賴，我們提出了一種時空方向注意力（STDA）機制，通過條帶注意力捕捉全局運動模式。此外，我們設計了一個時間幀圖推理模塊（TFRM），通過圖結構學習明確建模影片幀之間的時間一致性。為了增強情感語義控制，我們使用大型語言模型從真實影片中提取文本描述，作為高級語義指導。對於HDTF和MEAD數據集的實驗表明，我們的方法在嘴唇同步準確性、時間一致性和情感準確性方面優於現有方法。

##### **$\mathcal{S}^2$IT: Stepwise Syntax Integration Tuning for Large Language Models in Aspect Sentiment Quad Prediction**
2604.23296v1 by Bingfeng Chen, Chenjie Qiu, Yifeng Xie, Boyan Xu, Ruichu Cai, Zhifeng Hao

Aspect Sentiment Quad Prediction (ASQP) has seen significant advancements, largely driven by the powerful semantic understanding and generative capabilities of large language models (LLMs). However, while syntactic structure information has been proven effective in previous extractive paradigms, it remains underutilized in the generative paradigm of LLMs due to their limited reasoning capabilities. In this paper, we propose S^2IT, a novel Stepwise Syntax Integration Tuning framework that progressively integrates syntactic structure knowledge into LLMs through a multi-step tuning process. The training process is divided into three steps. S^2IT decomposes the quadruple generation task into two stages: 1) Global Syntax-guided Extraction and 2) Local Syntax-guided Classification, integrating both global and local syntactic structure information. Finally, Fine-grained Structural Tuning enhances the model's understanding of syntactic structures through the prediction of element links and node classification. Experiments demonstrate that S^2IT significantly improves state-of-the-art performance across multiple datasets. Our implementation will be open-sourced at https://github.com/DMIRLAB-Group/S2IT.

摘要：Aspect Sentiment Quad Prediction (ASQP) 已經取得了重大進展，這主要得益於大型語言模型 (LLMs) 強大的語義理解和生成能力。<lb/>然而，儘管語法結構信息在先前的提取範式中已被證明是有效的，但由於 LLMs 的推理能力有限，它在生成範式中仍然未被充分利用。<lb/>在本文中，我們提出了 S^2IT，一種新穎的逐步語法整合調整框架，通過多步調整過程逐步將語法結構知識整合到 LLMs 中。<lb/>訓練過程分為三個步驟。<lb/>S^2IT 將四元組生成任務分解為兩個階段：1) 全局語法引導提取和 2) 局部語法引導分類，整合全局和局部的語法結構信息。<lb/>最後，細粒度結構調整通過元素鏈接和節點分類的預測增強了模型對語法結構的理解。<lb/>實驗表明，S^2IT 在多個數據集上顯著提高了最先進的性能。<lb/>我們的實現將在 https://github.com/DMIRLAB-Group/S2IT 開源。

##### **From Similarity to Structure: Training-free LLM Context Compression with Hybrid Graph Priors**
2604.23277v1 by Yitian Zhou, Chaoning Zhang, Jiaquan Zhang, Zhenzhen Huang, Jinyu Guo, Sung-Ho Bae, Lik-Hang Lee, Caiyan Qin, Yang Yang

Long-context large language models remain computationally expensive to run and often fail to reliably process very long inputs, which makes context compression an important component of many systems. Existing compression approaches typically rely on trained compressors, dense retrieval-style selection, or heuristic trimming, and they often struggle to jointly preserve task relevance, topic coverage, and cross-sentence coherence under a strict token budget. To address this, we propose a training-free and model-agnostic compression framework that selects a compact set of sentences guided by structural graph priors. Our method constructs a sparse hybrid sentence graph that combines mutual k-NN semantic edges with short-range sequential edges, extracts a topic skeleton via clustering, and ranks sentences using an interpretable score that integrates task relevance, cluster representativeness, bridge centrality, and a cycle coverage cue. A budgeted greedy selection with redundancy suppression then produces a readable compressed context in original order. Experimental results on four datasets show that our approach is competitive with strong extractive and abstractive baselines, demonstrating larger gains on long-document benchmarks.

摘要：長文上下文的大型語言模型在運行上仍然計算成本高昂，並且往往無法可靠地處理非常長的輸入，這使得上下文壓縮成為許多系統的重要組成部分。現有的壓縮方法通常依賴於訓練過的壓縮器、密集檢索風格的選擇或啟發式修剪，並且在嚴格的標記預算下，往往難以共同保持任務相關性、主題覆蓋率和跨句子的一致性。為了解決這個問題，我們提出了一個無需訓練且與模型無關的壓縮框架，該框架根據結構圖的先驗選擇一組緊湊的句子。我們的方法構建了一個稀疏的混合句子圖，該圖結合了互相的 k-NN 語義邊和短距離的序列邊，通過聚類提取主題骨架，並使用一個可解釋的分數對句子進行排名，該分數整合了任務相關性、聚類代表性、橋接中心性和循環覆蓋提示。然後，預算內的貪婪選擇結合冗餘抑制，生成按原始順序排列的可讀壓縮上下文。在四個數據集上的實驗結果顯示，我們的方法在強提取和抽象基準上具有競爭力，並在長文檔基準上顯示出更大的增益。
